SNAP OPERATORS DOCUMENTATION
==================================================

OPERATOR: Aatsr.SST
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt Aatsr.SST [options] 

Description:
  Computes sea surface temperature (SST) from (A)ATSR products.


Source Options:
  -Ssource=<file>    The path of the (A)ATSR source product
                     This is a mandatory source.

Parameter Options:
  -Pdual=<boolean>                   Enables/disables generation of the dual-view SST
                                     Default value is 'true'.
  -PdualCoefficientsFile=<files>     Coefficient file for the dual-view SST
                                     Value must be one of 'AVERAGE_POLAR_DUAL_VIEW', 'AVERAGE_TEMPERATE_DUAL_VIEW', 'AVERAGE_TROPICAL_DUAL_VIEW', 'GRIDDED_POLAR_DUAL_VIEW', 'GRIDDED_TEMPERATE_DUAL_VIEW', 'GRIDDED_TROPICAL_DUAL_VIEW', 'GRIDDED_DUAL_VIEW_IPF'.
                                     Default value is 'AVERAGE_POLAR_DUAL_VIEW'.
  -PdualMaskExpression=<string>      ROI-mask used for the dual-view SST
                                     Default value is '!cloud_flags_nadir.LAND and !cloud_flags_nadir.CLOUDY and !cloud_flags_nadir.SUN_GLINT and !cloud_flags_fward.LAND and !cloud_flags_fward.CLOUDY and !cloud_flags_fward.SUN_GLINT'.
  -PinvalidSstValue=<float>          Value used to fill invalid SST pixels
                                     Default value is '-999.0f'.
  -Pnadir=<boolean>                  Enables/disables generation of the nadir-view SST
                                     Default value is 'true'.
  -PnadirCoefficientsFile=<files>    Coefficient file for the nadir-view SST
                                     Value must be one of 'AVERAGE_POLAR_SINGLE_VIEW', 'AVERAGE_TEMPERATE_SINGLE_VIEW', 'AVERAGE_TROPICAL_SINGLE_VIEW', 'GRIDDED_POLAR_SINGLE_VIEW', 'GRIDDED_TEMPERATE_SINGLE_VIEW', 'GRIDDED_TROPICAL_SINGLE_VIEW'.
                                     Default value is 'AVERAGE_POLAR_SINGLE_VIEW'.
  -PnadirMaskExpression=<string>     ROI-mask used for the nadir-view SST
                                     Default value is '!cloud_flags_nadir.LAND and !cloud_flags_nadir.CLOUDY and !cloud_flags_nadir.SUN_GLINT'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>Aatsr.SST</operator>
      <sources>
        <source>${source}</source>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <dual>boolean</dual>
        <dualCoefficientsFile>files</dualCoefficientsFile>
        <dualMaskExpression>string</dualMaskExpression>
        <nadir>boolean</nadir>
        <nadirCoefficientsFile>files</nadirCoefficientsFile>
        <nadirMaskExpression>string</nadirMaskExpression>
        <invalidSstValue>float</invalidSstValue>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

==================================================

OPERATOR: AATSR.Ungrid
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt AATSR.Ungrid [options] 

Description:
  Ungrids (A)ATSR L1B products and extracts geolocation and pixel field of view data.


Source Options:
  -SsourceProduct=<file>    (A)ATSR-1/2 source product (Envisat *.N1 format)
                            This is a mandatory source.

Parameter Options:
  -PcornerReferenceFlag=<boolean>     Choose the pixel coordinate reference point for use in the output file. 
                                      Check for Corner (default), un-check for Centre.
                                      Default value is 'true'.
  -PL1BCharacterisationFile=<file>    L1B characterisation file is needed to specify first forward pixel and first nadir pixel
  -PtopographicFlag=<boolean>         Option to apply topographic corrections to tie points
                                      Default value is 'false'.
  -PtopographyHomogenity=<double>     Distance (image coordinates) pixel can be from tie-point to have topo correction applied
                                      Default value is '0.05'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>AATSR.Ungrid</operator>
      <sources>
        <sourceProduct>${sourceProduct}</sourceProduct>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <L1BCharacterisationFile>file</L1BCharacterisationFile>
        <cornerReferenceFlag>boolean</cornerReferenceFlag>
        <topographicFlag>boolean</topographicFlag>
        <topographyHomogenity>double</topographyHomogenity>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

==================================================

OPERATOR: AdaptiveThresholding
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt AdaptiveThresholding [options] 

Description:
  Detect ships using Constant False Alarm Rate detector.


Source Options:
  -Ssource=<file>    Sets source 'source' to <filepath>.
                     This is a mandatory source.

Parameter Options:
  -PbackgroundWindowSizeInMeter=<double>    Background window size
                                            Default value is '800.0'.
  -PestimateBackground=<boolean>            Rough estimation of background threshold for quicker processing
                                            Default value is 'false'.
  -PguardWindowSizeInMeter=<double>         Guard window size
                                            Default value is '500.0'.
  -Ppfa=<double>                            Probability of false alarm
                                            Default value is '6.5'.
  -PtargetWindowSizeInMeter=<int>           Target window size
                                            Default value is '50'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>AdaptiveThresholding</operator>
      <sources>
        <source>${source}</source>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <targetWindowSizeInMeter>int</targetWindowSizeInMeter>
        <guardWindowSizeInMeter>double</guardWindowSizeInMeter>
        <backgroundWindowSizeInMeter>double</backgroundWindowSizeInMeter>
        <pfa>double</pfa>
        <estimateBackground>boolean</estimateBackground>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

OPERATOR: AddElevation
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt AddElevation [options] 

Description:
  Creates a DEM band


Source Options:
  -Ssource=<file>    Sets source 'source' to <filepath>.
                     This is a mandatory source.

Parameter Options:
  -PdemName=<string>                   The digital elevation model.
                                       Default value is 'SRTM 3Sec'.
  -PdemResamplingMethod=<string>       Sets parameter 'demResamplingMethod' to <string>.
                                       Default value is 'BICUBIC_INTERPOLATION'.
  -PelevationBandName=<string>         The elevation band name.
                                       Default value is 'elevation'.
  -PexternalDEMFile=<file>             Sets parameter 'externalDEMFile' to <file>.
  -PexternalDEMNoDataValue=<double>    Sets parameter 'externalDEMNoDataValue' to <double>.
                                       Default value is '0'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>AddElevation</operator>
      <sources>
        <source>${source}</source>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <demName>string</demName>
        <demResamplingMethod>string</demResamplingMethod>
        <externalDEMFile>file</externalDEMFile>
        <externalDEMNoDataValue>double</externalDEMNoDataValue>
        <elevationBandName>string</elevationBandName>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

OPERATOR: Apply-Orbit-File
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt Apply-Orbit-File [options] 

Description:
  Apply orbit file


Source Options:
  -Ssource=<file>    Sets source 'source' to <filepath>.
                     This is a mandatory source.

Parameter Options:
  -PcontinueOnFail=<boolean>    Sets parameter 'continueOnFail' to <boolean>.
                                Default value is 'false'.
  -PorbitType=<string>          Sets parameter 'orbitType' to <string>.
                                Value must be one of 'Sentinel Precise (Auto Download)', 'Sentinel Restituted (Auto Download)', 'DORIS Preliminary POR (ENVISAT)', 'DORIS Precise VOR (ENVISAT) (Auto Download)', 'DELFT Precise (ENVISAT, ERS1&2) (Auto Download)', 'PRARE Precise (ERS1&2) (Auto Download)', 'Kompsat5 Precise'.
                                Default value is 'Sentinel Precise (Auto Download)'.
  -PpolyDegree=<int>            Sets parameter 'polyDegree' to <int>.
                                Default value is '3'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>Apply-Orbit-File</operator>
      <sources>
        <source>${source}</source>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <orbitType>string</orbitType>
        <polyDegree>int</polyDegree>
        <continueOnFail>boolean</continueOnFail>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

OPERATOR: Arc.SST
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt Arc.SST [options] 

Description:
  Computes sea surface temperature (SST) from (A)ATSR and SLSTR products.


Source Options:
  -Ssource=<file>    The path of the (A)ATSR or SLSTR source product
                     This is a mandatory source.

Parameter Options:
  -Pasdi=<boolean>                      Enables/disables generation of ATSR Saharan Dust Index
                                        Default value is 'true'.
  -PasdiCoefficientsFile=<arcFiles>     Coefficient file for ASDI
                                        Value must be one of 'ASDI_ATSR1', 'ASDI_ATSR2', 'ASDI_AATSR'.
                                        Default value is 'ASDI_AATSR'.
  -PasdiMaskExpression=<string>         ROI-mask used for the ASDI
  -Pdual=<boolean>                      Enables/disables generation of the dual-view SST
                                        Default value is 'true'.
  -PdualCoefficientsFile=<arcFiles>     Coefficient file for the dual-view SST
                                        Value must be one of 'ARC_D2_ATSR1', 'ARC_D2_ATSR2', 'ARC_D2_AATSR', 'ARC_D2_SLSTR', 'ARC_D3_ATSR1', 'ARC_D3_ATSR2', 'ARC_D3_AATSR', 'ARC_D3_SLSTR'.
                                        Default value is 'ARC_D2_AATSR'.
  -PdualMaskExpression=<string>         ROI-mask used for the dual-view SST
  -PinvalidSstValue=<float>             Value used to fill invalid SST pixels
                                        Default value is '-999.0f'.
  -Pnadir=<boolean>                     Enables/disables generation of the nadir-view SST
                                        Default value is 'true'.
  -PnadirCoefficientsFile=<arcFiles>    Coefficient file for the nadir-view SST
                                        Value must be one of 'ARC_N2_ATSR1', 'ARC_N2_ATSR2', 'ARC_N2_AATSR', 'ARC_N2_SLSTR', 'ARC_N3_ATSR1', 'ARC_N3_ATSR2', 'ARC_N3_AATSR', 'ARC_N3_SLSTR'.
                                        Default value is 'ARC_N2_AATSR'.
  -PnadirMaskExpression=<string>        ROI-mask used for the nadir-view SST
  -PtcwvExpression=<string>             TCWV value to use in SST retrieval
                                        Default value is '30.0'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>Arc.SST</operator>
      <sources>
        <source>${source}</source>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <tcwvExpression>string</tcwvExpression>
        <asdi>boolean</asdi>
        <asdiCoefficientsFile>arcFiles</asdiCoefficientsFile>
        <asdiMaskExpression>string</asdiMaskExpression>
        <dual>boolean</dual>
        <dualCoefficientsFile>arcFiles</dualCoefficientsFile>
        <dualMaskExpression>string</dualMaskExpression>
        <nadir>boolean</nadir>
        <nadirCoefficientsFile>arcFiles</nadirCoefficientsFile>
        <nadirMaskExpression>string</nadirMaskExpression>
        <invalidSstValue>float</invalidSstValue>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

==================================================

OPERATOR: ArviOp
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt ArviOp [options] 

Description:
  Atmospherically Resistant Vegetation Index belongs to a family of indices with built-in atmospheric corrections.


Source Options:
  -Ssource=<file>    The source product.
                     This is a mandatory source.

Parameter Options:
  -PblueFactor=<float>         The value of the BLUE source band is multiplied by this value.
                               Default value is '1.0F'.
  -PblueSourceBand=<string>    The blue band for the ARVI computation. If not provided, the operator will try to find the best fitting band.
  -Pdownsampling=<string>      The method used for aggregation (downsampling to a coarser resolution).
                               Value must be one of 'First', 'Min', 'Max', 'Mean', 'Median'.
                               Default value is 'First'.
  -PgammaParameter=<float>     The gamma parameter is like a weighting function that depends on the aerosol type
                               Default value is '1.0F'.
  -PnirFactor=<float>          The value of the NIR source band is multiplied by this value.
                               Default value is '1.0F'.
  -PnirSourceBand=<string>     The near-infrared band for the ARVI computation. If not provided, the operator will try to find the best fitting band.
  -PredFactor=<float>          The value of the RED source band is multiplied by this value.
                               Default value is '1.0F'.
  -PredSourceBand=<string>     The red band for the ARVI computation. If not provided, the operator will try to find the best fitting band.
  -PresampleType=<string>      If selected band s differ in size, the resample method used before computing the index
                               Value must be one of 'None', 'Lowest resolution', 'Highest resolution'.
                               Default value is 'None'.
  -Pupsampling=<string>        The method used for interpolation (upsampling to a finer resolution).
                               Value must be one of 'Nearest', 'Bilinear', 'Bicubic'.
                               Default value is 'Nearest'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>ArviOp</operator>
      <sources>
        <source>${source}</source>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <resampleType>string</resampleType>
        <upsampling>string</upsampling>
        <downsampling>string</downsampling>
        <redFactor>float</redFactor>
        <blueFactor>float</blueFactor>
        <nirFactor>float</nirFactor>
        <gammaParameter>float</gammaParameter>
        <redSourceBand>string</redSourceBand>
        <blueSourceBand>string</blueSourceBand>
        <nirSourceBand>string</nirSourceBand>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

==================================================

OPERATOR: Azimuth-Shift-Estimation-ESD
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt Azimuth-Shift-Estimation-ESD [options] 

Description:
  Estimate azimuth offset for the whole image


Source Options:
  -Ssource=<file>    Sets source 'source' to <filepath>.
                     This is a mandatory source.

Parameter Options:
  -PcohThreshold=<double>        The coherence threshold for outlier removal
                                 Valid interval is (0, 1].
                                 Default value is '0.15'.
  -PnumBlocksPerOverlap=<int>    The number of windows per overlap for ESD
                                 Valid interval is [1, 20].
                                 Default value is '10'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>Azimuth-Shift-Estimation-ESD</operator>
      <sources>
        <source>${source}</source>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <cohThreshold>double</cohThreshold>
        <numBlocksPerOverlap>int</numBlocksPerOverlap>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

OPERATOR: AzimuthFilter
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt AzimuthFilter [options] 

Description:
  Azimuth Filter


Source Options:
  -SsourceProduct=<file>    Sets source 'sourceProduct' to <filepath>.
                            This is a mandatory source.

Parameter Options:
  -PalphaHamming=<float>      Weight for Hamming filter (1 is rectangular window)
                              Value must be one of '0.5', '0.75', '0.8', '0.9', '1'.
                              Default value is '0.75'.
  -PaziFilterOverlap=<int>    Overlap between filtering windows in azimuth direction [lines]
                              Value must be one of '0', '8', '16', '32', '64', '128', '256'.
                              Default value is '0'.
  -PfftLength=<int>           Length of filtering window
                              Value must be one of '64', '128', '256', '512', '1024', '2048'.
                              Default value is '256'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>AzimuthFilter</operator>
      <sources>
        <sourceProduct>${sourceProduct}</sourceProduct>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <fftLength>int</fftLength>
        <aziFilterOverlap>int</aziFilterOverlap>
        <alphaHamming>float</alphaHamming>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

OPERATOR: Back-Geocoding
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt Back-Geocoding [options] 

Description:
  Bursts co-registration using orbit and DEM


Parameter Options:
  -PdemName=<string>                         The digital elevation model.
                                             Default value is 'SRTM 3Sec'.
  -PdemResamplingMethod=<string>             Sets parameter 'demResamplingMethod' to <string>.
                                             Default value is 'BICUBIC_INTERPOLATION'.
  -PdisableReramp=<boolean>                  Sets parameter 'disableReramp' to <boolean>.
                                             Default value is 'false'.
  -PexternalDEMFile=<file>                   Sets parameter 'externalDEMFile' to <file>.
  -PexternalDEMNoDataValue=<double>          Sets parameter 'externalDEMNoDataValue' to <double>.
                                             Default value is '0'.
  -PmaskOutAreaWithoutElevation=<boolean>    Sets parameter 'maskOutAreaWithoutElevation' to <boolean>.
                                             Default value is 'true'.
  -PoutputDerampDemodPhase=<boolean>         Sets parameter 'outputDerampDemodPhase' to <boolean>.
                                             Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputRangeAzimuthOffset=<boolean>       Sets parameter 'outputRangeAzimuthOffset' to <boolean>.
                                             Default value is 'false'.
  -PresamplingType=<string>                  The method to be used when resampling the slave grid onto the master grid.
                                             Default value is 'BISINC_5_POINT_INTERPOLATION'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>Back-Geocoding</operator>
      <sources>
        <sourceProduct>${sourceProduct}</sourceProduct>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <demName>string</demName>
        <demResamplingMethod>string</demResamplingMethod>
        <externalDEMFile>file</externalDEMFile>
        <externalDEMNoDataValue>double</externalDEMNoDataValue>
        <resamplingType>string</resamplingType>
        <maskOutAreaWithoutElevation>boolean</maskOutAreaWithoutElevation>
        <outputRangeAzimuthOffset>boolean</outputRangeAzimuthOffset>
        <outputDerampDemodPhase>boolean</outputDerampDemodPhase>
        <disableReramp>boolean</disableReramp>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

OPERATOR: BandMaths
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt BandMaths [options] 

Description:
  Create a product with one or more bands using mathematical expressions.


Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>BandMaths</operator>
      <sources>
        <sourceProducts>${sourceProducts}</sourceProducts>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <targetBands>
          <targetBand>
            <name>string</name>
            <type>string</type>
            <expression>string</expression>
            <description>string</description>
            <unit>string</unit>
            <validExpression>string</validExpression>
            <noDataValue>double</noDataValue>
            <spectralBandIndex>integer</spectralBandIndex>
            <spectralWavelength>float</spectralWavelength>
            <angularValue>float</angularValue>
            <angularBandIndex>integer</angularBandIndex>
            <spectralBandwidth>float</spectralBandwidth>
            <scalingOffset>double</scalingOffset>
            <scalingFactor>double</scalingFactor>
          </targetBand>
          <_.002e../>
        </targetBands>
        <variables>
          <variable>
            <name>string</name>
            <type>string</type>
            <value>string</value>
          </variable>
          <_.002e../>
        </variables>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

                        Default value is '1'.

OPERATOR: BatchSnaphuUnwrapOp
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt BatchSnaphuUnwrapOp [options] 

Description:
  Downloads and executes SNAPHU on a set of two or more interferograms.


Source Options:
  -Ssource=<file>    Sets source 'source' to <filepath>.
                     This is a mandatory source.

Parameter Options:
  -PsnaphuInstallLocation=<file>       Directory to install the SNAPHU binary to
  -PsnaphuProcessingLocation=<file>    Directory that the Snaphu Export operator wrote to

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>BatchSnaphuUnwrapOp</operator>
      <sources>
        <source>${source}</source>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <snaphuProcessingLocation>file</snaphuProcessingLocation>
        <snaphuInstallLocation>file</snaphuInstallLocation>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

OPERATOR: Bi2Op
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt Bi2Op [options] 

Description:
  The second Brightness index represents the average of the brightness of a satellite image.


Source Options:
  -Ssource=<file>    The source product.
                     This is a mandatory source.

Parameter Options:
  -Pdownsampling=<string>       The method used for aggregation (downsampling to a coarser resolution).
                                Value must be one of 'First', 'Min', 'Max', 'Mean', 'Median'.
                                Default value is 'First'.
  -PgreenFactor=<float>         The value of the GREEN source band is multiplied by this value.
                                Default value is '1.0F'.
  -PgreenSourceBand=<string>    The green band for the BI2 computation. If not provided, the operator will try to find the best fitting band.
  -PnirFactor=<float>           The value of the NIR source band is multiplied by this value.
                                Default value is '1.0F'.
  -PnirSourceBand=<string>      The near-infrared band for the BI2 computation. If not provided, the operator will try to find the best fitting band.
  -PredFactor=<float>           The value of the RED source band is multiplied by this value.
                                Default value is '1.0F'.
  -PredSourceBand=<string>      The red band for the BI2 computation. If not provided, the operator will try to find the best fitting band.
  -PresampleType=<string>       If selected band s differ in size, the resample method used before computing the index
                                Value must be one of 'None', 'Lowest resolution', 'Highest resolution'.
                                Default value is 'None'.
  -Pupsampling=<string>         The method used for interpolation (upsampling to a finer resolution).
                                Value must be one of 'Nearest', 'Bilinear', 'Bicubic'.
                                Default value is 'Nearest'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>Bi2Op</operator>
      <sources>
        <source>${source}</source>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <resampleType>string</resampleType>
        <upsampling>string</upsampling>
        <downsampling>string</downsampling>
        <redFactor>float</redFactor>
        <greenFactor>float</greenFactor>
        <nirFactor>float</nirFactor>
        <redSourceBand>string</redSourceBand>
        <greenSourceBand>string</greenSourceBand>
        <nirSourceBand>string</nirSourceBand>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

==================================================

OPERATOR: Binning
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt Binning [options] 

Description:
  Performs spatial and temporal aggregation of pixel values into cells ('bins') of a planetary grid


Parameter Options:
  -PmaskExpr=<string>                                The band maths expression used to filter input pixels
  -PmaxDistanceOnEarth=<integer>                     Skips binning of sub-pixel if distance on earth to the center of the main-pixel is larger as this value. A value <=0 disables this check
                                                     Default value is '-1'.
  -PmetadataAggregatorName=<string>                  The type of metadata aggregation to be used. Possible values are:
                                                     'NAME': aggregate the name of each input product
                                                     'FIRST_HISTORY': aggregates all input product names and the processing history of the first product
                                                     'ALL_HISTORIES': aggregates all input product names and processing histories
                                                     Default value is 'NAME'.
  -PmetadataPropertiesFile=<file>                    The name of the file containing metadata key-value pairs (google "Java Properties file format").
                                                     Default value is './metadata.properties'.
  -PmetadataTemplateDir=<file>                       The name of the directory containing metadata templates (google "Apache Velocity VTL format").
                                                     Default value is '.'.
  -PminDataHour=<double>                             A sensor-dependent constant given in hours of a day (0 to 24)
                                                     at which a sensor has a minimum number of observations at the date line (the 180 degree meridian).
                                                     Only used if parameter 'dataDayMode' is set to 'SPATIOTEMPORAL_DATADAY'. This is usually the equator crossing time (ECT)
                                                     Valid interval is [0,24].
  -PnumRows=<int>                                    Number of rows in the (global) planetary grid. Must be even.
                                                     Default value is '2160'.
  -PoutputBinnedData=<boolean>                       If true, a SeaDAS-style, binned data NetCDF file is written in addition to the
                                                     target product. The output file name will be {target}-bins.nc
                                                     Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputFile=<string>                              Sets parameter 'outputFile' to <string>.
  -PoutputFormat=<string>                            Sets parameter 'outputFormat' to <string>.
                                                     Default value is 'BEAM-DIMAP'.
  -PoutputMappedProduct=<boolean>                    If true, a mapped product is written. Set this to 'false' if only a binned product is needed.
                                                     Default value is 'true'.
  -PoutputType=<string>                              Sets parameter 'outputType' to <string>.
                                                     Value must be one of 'Product', 'RGB', 'Grey'.
                                                     Default value is 'Product'.
  -PperiodDuration=<double>                          Duration of the binning period in days.
  -PplanetaryGridClass=<string>                      Sets parameter 'planetaryGridClass' to <string>.
                                                     Default value is 'org.esa.snap.binning.support.SEAGrid'.
  -Pregion=<geometry>                                The considered geographical region as a geometry in well-known text format (WKT).
                                                     If not given, the geographical region will be computed according to the extents of the input products.
  -PsourceGraphPaths=<string,string,string,...>      A comma-separated list of file paths specifying the source graphs.
                                                     Each path may contain the wildcards '**' (matches recursively any directory),
                                                     '*' (matches any character sequence in path names) and
                                                     '?' (matches any single character).
  -PsourceProductFormat=<string>                     The common product format of all source products.
                                                     This parameter is optional and may be used in conjunction with
                                                     parameter 'sourceProductPaths'. Can be set if multiple reader are 
                                                     available for the source files and a specific one shall be used.Try "NetCDF-CF", "GeoTIFF", "BEAM-DIMAP", or "ENVISAT", etc.
  -PsourceProductPaths=<string,string,string,...>    A comma-separated list of file paths specifying the source products.
                                                     Each path may contain the wildcards '**' (matches recursively any directory),
                                                     '*' (matches any character sequence in path names) and
                                                     '?' (matches any single character).
  -PstartDateTime=<string>                           The UTC start date of the binning period.
                                                     The format is either 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss' or 'yyyy-MM-dd'.
                                                      If only the date part is given, the time 00:00:00 is assumed.
                                                     Pattern for valid values is '\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}(\s\d{2}:\d{2}:\d{2})?'.
  -PsuperSampling=<integer>                          The square of the number of pixels used for super-sampling an input pixel into multiple sub-pixels
                                                     Default value is '1'.
  -PtimeFilterMethod=<timeFilterMethod>              The method that is used to decide which source pixels are used with respect to their observation time.
                                                     'NONE': ignore pixel observation time, use all source pixels.
                                                     'TIME_RANGE': use all pixels that have been acquired in the given binning period.
                                                     'SPATIOTEMPORAL_DATA_DAY': use a sensor-dependent, spatial "data-day" definition with the goal
                                                     to minimise the time between the first and last observation contributing to the same bin in the given binning period.
                                                     The decision, whether a source pixel contributes to a bin or not, is a function of the pixel's observation longitude and time.
                                                     Requires the parameter 'minDataHour'.
                                                     Default value is 'NONE'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>Binning</operator>
      <sources>
        <sourceProducts>${sourceProducts}</sourceProducts>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <sourceProductPaths>string,string,string,...</sourceProductPaths>
        <sourceProductFormat>string</sourceProductFormat>
        <sourceGraphPaths>string,string,string,...</sourceGraphPaths>
        <region>geometry</region>
        <startDateTime>string</startDateTime>
        <periodDuration>double</periodDuration>
        <timeFilterMethod>timeFilterMethod</timeFilterMethod>
        <minDataHour>double</minDataHour>
        <numRows>int</numRows>
        <superSampling>integer</superSampling>
        <maxDistanceOnEarth>integer</maxDistanceOnEarth>
        <maskExpr>string</maskExpr>
        <variables>
          <variable>
            <name>string</name>
            <expr>string</expr>
            <validExpr>string</validExpr>
          </variable>
          <_.002e../>
        </variables>
        <aggregators>aggregatorConfig,aggregatorConfig,aggregatorConfig,...</aggregators>
        <postProcessor/>
        <outputType>string</outputType>
        <outputFile>string</outputFile>
        <outputFormat>string</outputFormat>
        <outputBands>
          <band>
            <index>string</index>
            <name>string</name>
            <minValue>string</minValue>
            <maxValue>string</maxValue>
          </band>
          <_.002e../>
        </outputBands>
        <productCustomizer/>
        <outputBinnedData>boolean</outputBinnedData>
        <outputMappedProduct>boolean</outputMappedProduct>
        <metadataPropertiesFile>file</metadataPropertiesFile>
        <metadataTemplateDir>file</metadataTemplateDir>
        <metadataAggregatorName>string</metadataAggregatorName>
        <planetaryGridClass>string</planetaryGridClass>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

  -PcomputeFcover=<boolean>    Compute FVC (Fraction of Vegetation Cover)
                               Default value is 'true'.
  -PcomputeLAI=<boolean>       Compute LAI (Leaf Area Index)
                               Default value is 'true'.
  -Psensor=<string>            Sensor
                               Value must be one of 'S2A_10m', 'S2B_10m', 'S2C_10m'.
                               Default value is 'S2A_10m'.

        <computeFcover>boolean</computeFcover>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

----------------------------------------

OPERATOR: c2rcc.landsat8
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt c2rcc.landsat8 [options] 

Description:
  Performs atmospheric correction and IOP retrieval with uncertainties on Landsat-8 L1 data products.


Source Options:
  -SncepEndProduct=<file>         The second product providing air pressure values for pressure interpolation. Use either the TOMSOMI and NCEP products or the atmosphericAuxdataPath to as source for ozone and air pressure.
                                  This is an optional source.
  -SncepStartProduct=<file>       The first product providing air pressure values for pressure interpolation. Use either the TOMSOMI and NCEP products or the atmosphericAuxdataPath to as source for ozone and air pressure.
                                  This is an optional source.
  -SsourceProduct=<file>          Landsat 8 source product.
                                  This is a mandatory source.
  -StomsomiEndProduct=<file>      The second product providing ozone values for ozone interpolation. Use either the TOMSOMI and NCEP products or the atmosphericAuxdataPath to as source for ozone and air pressure.
                                  This is an optional source.
  -StomsomiStartProduct=<file>    The first product providing ozone values for ozone interpolation. Use either the TOMSOMI and NCEP products or the atmosphericAuxdataPath to as source for ozone and air pressure.
                                  This is an optional source.

Parameter Options:
  -PalternativeNNPath=<string>                    Path to an alternative set of neuronal nets. Use this to replace the standard set of neuronal nets.
  -PatmosphericAuxDataPath=<string>               Path to the atmospheric auxiliary data directory. Use either this or the specified products on the I/O Parameters tab. If the auxiliary data is not available at this path, the data will automatically be downloaded.
  -PCHLexp=<double>                               Chlorophyll exponent ( CHL = iop_apig^CHLexp * CHLfac).
                                                  Default value is '1.04'.
  -PCHLfac=<double>                               Chlorophyll factor ( CHL = iop_apig^CHLexp * CHLfac).
                                                  Default value is '21.0'.
  -PdemName=<string>                              The digital elevation model.
                                                  Value must be one of 'Copernicus 90m Global DEM', 'Copernicus 30m Global DEM', 'GETASSE30'.
                                                  Default value is 'Copernicus 90m Global DEM'.
  -PderiveRwFromPathAndTransmittance=<boolean>    Alternative way of calculating water reflectance. Still experimental.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -Pelevation=<double>                            Used as fallback if elevation could not be taken from DEM.
                                                  Valid interval is (0, 8500).
                                                  Default value is '0'.
                                                  Parameter unit is 'm'.
  -PnetSet=<string>                               Set of neuronal nets for algorithm.
                                                  Value must be one of 'C2RCC-Nets', 'C2X-Nets'.
                                                  Default value is 'C2RCC-Nets'.
  -PoutputAcReflectance=<boolean>                 Sets parameter 'outputAcReflectance' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'true'.
  -PoutputAsRrs=<boolean>                         Write remote sensing reflectances instead of water leaving reflectances.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputKd=<boolean>                            Sets parameter 'outputKd' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'true'.
  -PoutputOos=<boolean>                           Sets parameter 'outputOos' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputRhown=<boolean>                         Sets parameter 'outputRhown' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'true'.
  -PoutputRpath=<boolean>                         Sets parameter 'outputRpath' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputRtoa=<boolean>                          Sets parameter 'outputRtoa' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'true'.
  -PoutputRtosaGc=<boolean>                       Sets parameter 'outputRtosaGc' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputRtosaGcAann=<boolean>                   Sets parameter 'outputRtosaGcAann' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputTdown=<boolean>                         Sets parameter 'outputTdown' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputTup=<boolean>                           Sets parameter 'outputTup' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputUncertainties=<boolean>                 Sets parameter 'outputUncertainties' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'true'.
  -Pozone=<double>                                The value used as ozone if not provided by auxiliary data.
                                                  Valid interval is (0, 1000).
                                                  Default value is '330'.
                                                  Parameter unit is 'DU'.
  -Ppress=<double>                                The surface air pressure at sea level if not provided by auxiliary data.
                                                  Valid interval is (800, 1040).
                                                  Default value is '1000'.
                                                  Parameter unit is 'hPa'.
  -Psalinity=<double>                             The value used as salinity for the scene.
                                                  Valid interval is (0.000028, 43).
                                                  Default value is '35.0'.
                                                  Parameter unit is 'PSU'.
  -Ptemperature=<double>                          The value used as temperature for the scene.
                                                  Valid interval is (0.000111, 36).
                                                  Default value is '15.0'.
                                                  Parameter unit is 'C'.
  -PthresholdAcReflecOos=<double>                 Threshold for out of scope of nn training dataset flag for atmospherically corrected reflectances
                                                  Default value is '0.1'.
  -PthresholdCloudTDown865=<double>               Threshold for cloud test based on downwelling transmittance @865
                                                  Default value is '0.955'.
  -PthresholdRtosaOOS=<double>                    Threshold for out of scope of nn training dataset flag for gas corrected top-of-atmosphere reflectances.
                                                  Default value is '0.05'.
  -PTSMexp=<double>                               TSM exponent (TSM = TSMfac * iop_btot^TSMexp).
                                                  Default value is '3.1'.
  -PTSMfac=<double>                               TSM factor (TSM = TSMfac * iop_btot^TSMexp).
                                                  Default value is '1.72'.
  -PvalidPixelExpression=<string>                 Defines the pixels which are valid for processing.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>c2rcc.landsat8</operator>
      <sources>
        <sourceProduct>${sourceProduct}</sourceProduct>
        <tomsomiStartProduct>${tomsomiStartProduct}</tomsomiStartProduct>
        <tomsomiEndProduct>${tomsomiEndProduct}</tomsomiEndProduct>
        <ncepStartProduct>${ncepStartProduct}</ncepStartProduct>
        <ncepEndProduct>${ncepEndProduct}</ncepEndProduct>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <validPixelExpression>string</validPixelExpression>
        <salinity>double</salinity>
        <temperature>double</temperature>
        <ozone>double</ozone>
        <press>double</press>
        <elevation>double</elevation>
        <TSMfac>double</TSMfac>
        <TSMexp>double</TSMexp>
        <CHLexp>double</CHLexp>
        <CHLfac>double</CHLfac>
        <thresholdRtosaOOS>double</thresholdRtosaOOS>
        <thresholdAcReflecOos>double</thresholdAcReflecOos>
        <thresholdCloudTDown865>double</thresholdCloudTDown865>
        <atmosphericAuxDataPath>string</atmosphericAuxDataPath>
        <alternativeNNPath>string</alternativeNNPath>
        <netSet>string</netSet>
        <outputAsRrs>boolean</outputAsRrs>
        <deriveRwFromPathAndTransmittance>boolean</deriveRwFromPathAndTransmittance>
        <demName>string</demName>
        <outputRtoa>boolean</outputRtoa>
        <outputRtosaGc>boolean</outputRtosaGc>
        <outputRtosaGcAann>boolean</outputRtosaGcAann>
        <outputRpath>boolean</outputRpath>
        <outputTdown>boolean</outputTdown>
        <outputTup>boolean</outputTup>
        <outputAcReflectance>boolean</outputAcReflectance>
        <outputRhown>boolean</outputRhown>
        <outputOos>boolean</outputOos>
        <outputKd>boolean</outputKd>
        <outputUncertainties>boolean</outputUncertainties>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

==================================================

OPERATOR: c2rcc.meris
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt c2rcc.meris [options] 

Description:
  Performs atmospheric correction and IOP retrieval with uncertainties on MERIS L1b data products.


Source Options:
  -SncepEndProduct=<file>         The second product providing air pressure values for pressure interpolation. Use either the TOMSOMI and NCEP products or the atmosphericAuxdataPath to as source for ozone and air pressure.
                                  This is an optional source.
  -SncepStartProduct=<file>       The first product providing air pressure values for pressure interpolation. Use either the TOMSOMI and NCEP products or the atmosphericAuxdataPath to as source for ozone and air pressure.
                                  This is an optional source.
  -SsourceProduct=<file>          MERIS L1b source product.
                                  This is a mandatory source.
  -StomsomiEndProduct=<file>      The second product providing ozone values for ozone interpolation. Use either the TOMSOMI and NCEP products or the atmosphericAuxdataPath to as source for ozone and air pressure.
                                  This is an optional source.
  -StomsomiStartProduct=<file>    The first product providing ozone values for ozone interpolation. Use either the TOMSOMI and NCEP products or the atmosphericAuxdataPath to as source for ozone and air pressure.
                                  This is an optional source.

Parameter Options:
  -PalternativeNNPath=<string>                    Path to an alternative set of neuronal nets. Use this to replace the standard set of neuronal nets.
  -PatmosphericAuxDataPath=<string>               Path to the atmospheric auxiliary data directory. Use either this or the specified products on the I/O Parameters tab. If the auxiliary data is not available at this path, the data will automatically be downloaded.
  -PCHLexp=<double>                               Chlorophyll exponent ( CHL = iop_apig^CHLexp * CHLfac).
                                                  Default value is '1.04'.
  -PCHLfac=<double>                               Chlorophyll factor ( CHL = iop_apig^CHLexp * CHLfac).
                                                  Default value is '21.0'.
  -PdemName=<string>                              The digital elevation model. Default uses product's 'dem_alt' band
                                                  Value must be one of '', 'Copernicus 30m Global DEM', 'Copernicus 90m Global DEM', 'GETASSE30'.
  -PderiveRwFromPathAndTransmittance=<boolean>    Alternative way of calculating water reflectance. Still experimental.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PnetSet=<string>                               Set of neuronal nets for algorithm.
                                                  Value must be one of 'C2RCC-Nets', 'C2X-Nets'.
                                                  Default value is 'C2RCC-Nets'.
  -PoutputAcReflectance=<boolean>                 Sets parameter 'outputAcReflectance' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'true'.
  -PoutputAsRrs=<boolean>                         Write remote sensing reflectances instead of water leaving reflectances.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputKd=<boolean>                            Sets parameter 'outputKd' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'true'.
  -PoutputOos=<boolean>                           Sets parameter 'outputOos' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputRhown=<boolean>                         Sets parameter 'outputRhown' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'true'.
  -PoutputRpath=<boolean>                         Sets parameter 'outputRpath' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputRtoa=<boolean>                          Sets parameter 'outputRtoa' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'true'.
  -PoutputRtosaGc=<boolean>                       Sets parameter 'outputRtosaGc' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputRtosaGcAann=<boolean>                   Sets parameter 'outputRtosaGcAann' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputTdown=<boolean>                         Sets parameter 'outputTdown' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputTup=<boolean>                           Sets parameter 'outputTup' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputUncertainties=<boolean>                 Sets parameter 'outputUncertainties' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'true'.
  -Pozone=<double>                                The value used as ozone if not provided by auxiliary data.
                                                  Valid interval is (0, 1000).
                                                  Default value is '330'.
                                                  Parameter unit is 'DU'.
  -Ppress=<double>                                The surface air pressure at sea level if not provided by auxiliary data.
                                                  Valid interval is (800, 1040).
                                                  Default value is '1000'.
                                                  Parameter unit is 'hPa'.
  -Psalinity=<double>                             The value used as salinity for the scene.
                                                  Valid interval is (0.000028, 43).
                                                  Default value is '35.0'.
                                                  Parameter unit is 'PSU'.
  -Ptemperature=<double>                          The value used as temperature for the scene.
                                                  Valid interval is (0.000111, 36).
                                                  Default value is '15.0'.
                                                  Parameter unit is 'C'.
  -PthresholdAcReflecOos=<double>                 Threshold for out of scope of nn training dataset flag for atmospherically corrected reflectances.
                                                  Default value is '0.1'.
  -PthresholdCloudTDown865=<double>               Threshold for cloud test based on downwelling transmittance @865.
                                                  Default value is '0.955'.
  -PthresholdRtosaOOS=<double>                    Threshold for out of scope of nn training dataset flag for gas corrected top-of-atmosphere reflectances.
                                                  Default value is '0.003'.
  -PTSMexp=<double>                               TSM exponent (TSM = TSMfac * iop_btot^TSMexp).
                                                  Default value is '3.1'.
  -PTSMfac=<double>                               TSM factor (TSM = TSMfac * iop_btot^TSMexp).
                                                  Default value is '1.72'.
  -PuseDefaultSolarFlux=<boolean>                 If 'false', use solar flux from source product
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PuseEcmwfAuxData=<boolean>                     If selected, the ECMWF auxiliary data (ozon, air pressure) of the source product is used
                                                  Default value is 'true'.
  -PvalidPixelExpression=<string>                 Defines the pixels which are valid for processing.
                                                  Default value is '!l1_flags.INVALID && !l1_flags.LAND_OCEAN'.

OPERATOR: c2rcc.meris4
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt c2rcc.meris4 [options] 

Description:
  Performs atmospheric correction and IOP retrieval with uncertainties on MERIS L1b data products from the 4th reprocessing.


Source Options:
  -SncepEndProduct=<file>         The second product providing air pressure values for pressure interpolation. Use either the TOMSOMI and NCEP products or the atmosphericAuxdataPath to as source for ozone and air pressure.
                                  This is an optional source.
  -SncepStartProduct=<file>       The first product providing air pressure values for pressure interpolation. Use either the TOMSOMI and NCEP products or the atmosphericAuxdataPath to as source for ozone and air pressure.
                                  This is an optional source.
  -SsourceProduct=<file>          MERIS L1b source product.
                                  This is a mandatory source.
  -StomsomiEndProduct=<file>      The second product providing ozone values for ozone interpolation. Use either the TOMSOMI and NCEP products or the atmosphericAuxdataPath to as source for ozone and air pressure.
                                  This is an optional source.
  -StomsomiStartProduct=<file>    The first product providing ozone values for ozone interpolation. Use either the TOMSOMI and NCEP products or the atmosphericAuxdataPath to as source for ozone and air pressure.
                                  This is an optional source.

Parameter Options:
  -PalternativeNNPath=<string>                    Path to an alternative set of neuronal nets. Use this to replace the standard set of neuronal nets with the ones in the given directory.
  -PatmosphericAuxDataPath=<string>               Path to the atmospheric auxiliary data directory. Use either this or the specified products on the I/O Parameters tab. If the auxiliary data is not available at this path, the data will automatically be downloaded.
  -PCHLexp=<double>                               Chlorophyll exponent ( CHL = iop_apig^CHLexp * CHLfac).
                                                  Default value is '1.04'.
  -PCHLfac=<double>                               Chlorophyll factor ( CHL = iop_apig^CHLexp * CHLfac).
                                                  Default value is '21.0'.
  -PdemName=<string>                              The digital elevation model. Default uses product's 'dem_alt' band
                                                  Value must be one of '', 'Copernicus 30m Global DEM', 'Copernicus 90m Global DEM', 'GETASSE30'.
  -PderiveRwFromPathAndTransmittance=<boolean>    Alternative way of calculating water reflectance. Still experimental.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PnetSet=<string>                               Set of neuronal nets for algorithm.
                                                  Value must be one of 'C2RCC-Nets', 'C2X-Nets'.
                                                  Default value is 'C2RCC-Nets'.
  -PoutputAcReflectance=<boolean>                 Sets parameter 'outputAcReflectance' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'true'.
  -PoutputAsRrs=<boolean>                         Write remote sensing reflectances instead of water leaving reflectances.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputKd=<boolean>                            Sets parameter 'outputKd' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'true'.
  -PoutputOos=<boolean>                           Sets parameter 'outputOos' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputRhown=<boolean>                         Sets parameter 'outputRhown' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'true'.
  -PoutputRpath=<boolean>                         Sets parameter 'outputRpath' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputRtoa=<boolean>                          Sets parameter 'outputRtoa' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'true'.
  -PoutputRtosaGc=<boolean>                       Sets parameter 'outputRtosaGc' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputRtosaGcAann=<boolean>                   Sets parameter 'outputRtosaGcAann' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputTdown=<boolean>                         Sets parameter 'outputTdown' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputTup=<boolean>                           Sets parameter 'outputTup' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputUncertainties=<boolean>                 Sets parameter 'outputUncertainties' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'true'.
  -Pozone=<double>                                The value used as ozone if not provided by auxiliary data.
                                                  Valid interval is (0, 1000).
                                                  Default value is '330'.
                                                  Parameter unit is 'DU'.
  -Ppress=<double>                                The surface air pressure at sea level if not provided by auxiliary data.
                                                  Valid interval is (800, 1040).
                                                  Default value is '1000'.
                                                  Parameter unit is 'hPa'.
  -Psalinity=<double>                             The value used as salinity for the scene.
                                                  Valid interval is (0.000028, 43).
                                                  Default value is '35.0'.
                                                  Parameter unit is 'PSU'.
  -Ptemperature=<double>                          The value used as temperature for the scene.
                                                  Valid interval is (0.000111, 36).
                                                  Default value is '15.0'.
                                                  Parameter unit is 'C'.
  -PthresholdAcReflecOos=<double>                 Threshold for out of scope of nn training dataset flag for atmospherically corrected reflectances.
                                                  Default value is '0.1'.
  -PthresholdCloudTDown865=<double>               Threshold for cloud test based on downwelling transmittance @865.
                                                  Default value is '0.955'.
  -PthresholdRtosaOOS=<double>                    Threshold for out of scope of nn training dataset flag for gas corrected top-of-atmosphere reflectances.
                                                  Default value is '0.003'.
  -PTSMexp=<double>                               TSM exponent (TSM = TSMfac * iop_btot^TSMexp).
                                                  Default value is '3.1'.
  -PTSMfac=<double>                               TSM factor (TSM = TSMfac * iop_btot^TSMexp).
                                                  Default value is '1.72'.
  -PuseEcmwfAuxData=<boolean>                     If selected, the ECMWF auxiliary data (total_ozone, sea_level_pressure) of the source product is used
                                                  Default value is 'true'.
  -PvalidPixelExpression=<string>                 Defines the pixels which are valid for processing.
                                                  Default value is '!quality_flags.invalid && (!quality_flags.land || quality_flags.fresh_inland_water)'.

----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt c2rcc.modis [options] 

Description:

  -SncepStartProduct=<file>       The first product providing air pressure values for pressure interpolation. Use either the TOMSOMI and NCEP products or the atmosphericAuxdataPath to as source for ozone and air pressure.
                                  This is an optional source.

                                  This is a mandatory source.

                                  This is an optional source.

                                  This is an optional source.

Parameter Options:
  -PatmosphericAuxDataPath=<string>    Path to the atmospheric auxiliary data directory. Use either this or the specific products. If the auxiliary data needed for interpolation is not available in this path, the data will automatically downloaded.
  -PoutputAngles=<boolean>             Sets parameter 'outputAngles' to <boolean>.
                                       Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputAsRrs=<boolean>              Reflectance values in the target product shall be either written as remote sensing or water leaving reflectances
                                       Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputRtosa=<boolean>              Sets parameter 'outputRtosa' to <boolean>.
                                       Default value is 'false'.
  -Pozone=<double>                     The value used as ozone if not provided by auxiliary data

                                       Parameter unit is 'DU'.
  -Ppress=<double>                     The surface air pressure at sea level if not provided by auxiliary data
                                       Valid interval is (800, 1040).
                                       Default value is '1000'.
                                       Parameter unit is 'hPa'.
  -Psalinity=<double>                  The value used as salinity for the scene
                                       Valid interval is (0.000028, 43).
                                       Default value is '35.0'.
                                       Parameter unit is 'PSU'.
  -Ptemperature=<double>               The value used as temperature for the scene
                                       Valid interval is (0.000111, 36).
                                       Default value is '15.0'.
                                       Parameter unit is 'C'.
  -PvalidPixelExpression=<string>      Defines the pixels which are valid for processing
                                       Default value is '!(l2_flags.LAND ||  max(rhot_412,max(rhot_443,max(rhot_488,max(rhot_531,max(rhot_547,max(rhot_555,max(rhot_667,max(rhot_678,max(rhot_748,rhot_869)))))))))>0.25)'.

                                  This is a mandatory source.

                                  This is an optional source.

  -PalternativeNNPath=<string>                    Path to an alternative set of neuronal nets. Use this to replace the standard set of neuronal nets.
  -PatmosphericAuxDataPath=<string>               Path to the atmospheric auxiliary data directory. Use either this or the specified products on the I/O Parameters tab. If the auxiliary data is not available at this path, the data will automatically be downloaded.
  -PCHLexp=<double>                               Chlorophyll exponent ( CHL = iop_apig^CHLexp * CHLfac).
                                                  Default value is '1.04'.

  -PderiveRwFromPathAndTransmittance=<boolean>    Alternative way of calculating water reflectance. Still experimental.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.

                                                  Valid interval is (0, 8500).

  -PoutputRpath=<boolean>                         Sets parameter 'outputRpath' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputRtoa=<boolean>                          Sets parameter 'outputRtoa' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'true'.
  -PoutputRtosaGc=<boolean>                       Sets parameter 'outputRtosaGc' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputRtosaGcAann=<boolean>                   Sets parameter 'outputRtosaGcAann' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputTdown=<boolean>                         Sets parameter 'outputTdown' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputTup=<boolean>                           Sets parameter 'outputTup' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputUncertainties=<boolean>                 Sets parameter 'outputUncertainties' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'true'.

                                                  Default value is '330'.
                                                  Parameter unit is 'DU'.
  -Ppress=<double>                                The surface air pressure at sea level if not provided by auxiliary data.
                                                  Valid interval is (800, 1040).
                                                  Default value is '1000'.
                                                  Parameter unit is 'hPa'.
  -Psalinity=<double>                             The value used as salinity for the scene.
                                                  Valid interval is (0.000028, 43).
                                                  Default value is '35.0'.
                                                  Parameter unit is 'PSU'.
  -Ptemperature=<double>                          The value used as temperature for the scene.
                                                  Valid interval is (0.000111, 36).
                                                  Default value is '15.0'.
                                                  Parameter unit is 'C'.
  -PthresholdAcReflecOos=<double>                 Threshold for out of scope of nn training dataset flag for atmospherically corrected reflectances
                                                  Default value is '0.1'.
  -PthresholdCloudTDown865=<double>               Threshold for cloud test based on downwelling transmittance @865
                                                  Default value is '0.955'.
  -PthresholdRtosaOOS=<double>                    Threshold for out of scope of nn training dataset flag for gas corrected top-of-atmosphere reflectances
                                                  Default value is '0.05'.
  -PTSMexp=<double>                               TSM exponent (TSM = TSMfac * iop_btot^TSMexp).
                                                  Default value is '0.942'.
  -PTSMfac=<double>                               TSM factor (TSM = TSMfac * iop_btot^TSMexp).
                                                  Default value is '1.06'.
  -PuseEcmwfAuxData=<boolean>                     Use ECMWF auxiliary data (msl and tco3) from the source product, if available.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PvalidPixelExpression=<string>                 Defines the pixels which are valid for processing.
                                                  Default value is 'B8 > 0 && B8 < 0.1'.

----------------------------------------

  -SsourceProduct=<file>          OLCI L1b source product.
                                  This is a mandatory source.
  -StomsomiEndProduct=<file>      The second product providing ozone values for ozone interpolation. Use either the TOMSOMI and NCEP products or the atmosphericAuxdataPath to as source for ozone and air pressure.
                                  This is an optional source.
  -StomsomiStartProduct=<file>    The first product providing ozone values for ozone interpolation. Use either the TOMSOMI and NCEP products or the atmosphericAuxdataPath to as source for ozone and air pressure.
                                  This is an optional source.

Parameter Options:
  -PalternativeNNPath=<string>                    Path to an alternative set of neuronal nets. Use this to replace the standard set of neuronal nets.
  -PatmosphericAuxDataPath=<string>               Path to the atmospheric auxiliary data directory. Use either this or the specified products on the I/O Parameters tab. If the auxiliary data is not available at this path, the data will automatically be downloaded.
  -PCHLexp=<double>                               Chlorophyll exponent ( CHL = iop_apig^CHLexp * CHLfac).
                                                  Default value is '1.04'.
  -PCHLfac=<double>                               Chlorophyll factor ( CHL = iop_apig^CHLexp * CHLfac).
                                                  Default value is '21.0'.
  -PdemName=<string>                              The digital elevation model. Default uses product's 'altitude' band
                                                  Value must be one of '', 'Copernicus 30m Global DEM', 'Copernicus 90m Global DEM', 'GETASSE30'.
  -PderiveRwFromPathAndTransmittance=<boolean>    Alternative way of calculating water reflectance. Still experimental.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputAcReflectance=<boolean>                 Sets parameter 'outputAcReflectance' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'true'.
  -PoutputAsRrs=<boolean>                         Write remote sensing reflectances instead of water leaving reflectances.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputKd=<boolean>                            Sets parameter 'outputKd' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'true'.
  -PoutputOos=<boolean>                           Sets parameter 'outputOos' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputRhown=<boolean>                         Sets parameter 'outputRhown' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'true'.
  -PoutputRpath=<boolean>                         Sets parameter 'outputRpath' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputRtoa=<boolean>                          Sets parameter 'outputRtoa' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'true'.
  -PoutputRtosaGc=<boolean>                       Sets parameter 'outputRtosaGc' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputRtosaGcAann=<boolean>                   Sets parameter 'outputRtosaGcAann' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputTdown=<boolean>                         Sets parameter 'outputTdown' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputTup=<boolean>                           Sets parameter 'outputTup' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputUncertainties=<boolean>                 Sets parameter 'outputUncertainties' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'true'.
  -Pozone=<double>                                The value used as ozone if not provided by auxiliary data.
                                                  Valid interval is (0, 1000).
                                                  Default value is '330'.
                                                  Parameter unit is 'DU'.
  -Ppress=<double>                                The surface air pressure at sea level if not provided by auxiliary data.
                                                  Valid interval is (800, 1040).
                                                  Default value is '1000'.
                                                  Parameter unit is 'hPa'.
  -Psalinity=<double>                             The value used as salinity for the scene.
                                                  Valid interval is (0.000028, 43).
                                                  Default value is '35.0'.
                                                  Parameter unit is 'PSU'.
  -Ptemperature=<double>                          The value used as temperature for the scene.
                                                  Valid interval is (0.000111, 36).
                                                  Default value is '15.0'.
                                                  Parameter unit is 'C'.
  -PthresholdAcReflecOos=<double>                 Threshold for nn training dataset out of scope flag for atmospherically corrected reflectances.
                                                  Default value is '0.15'.
  -PthresholdCloudTDown865=<double>               Threshold for cloud test based on downwelling transmittance @865.
                                                  Default value is '0.955'.
  -PthresholdRtosaOOS=<double>                    Threshold for nn training dataset out of scope flag for gas corrected top-of-atmosphere reflectances.
                                                  Default value is '0.01'.
  -PTSMexp=<double>                               TSM exponent (TSM = TSMfac * iop_btot^TSMexp).
                                                  Default value is '0.942'.
  -PTSMfac=<double>                               TSM factor (TSM = TSMfac * iop_btot^TSMexp).
                                                  Default value is '1.06'.
  -PuseEcmwfAuxData=<boolean>                     Use ECMWF auxiliary data (total_ozone, sea_level_pressure) from the source product.
                                                  Default value is 'true'.
  -PvalidPixelExpression=<string>                 Defines the pixels which are valid for processing.
                                                  Default value is '!quality_flags.invalid && (!quality_flags.land || quality_flags.fresh_inland_water)'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>c2rcc.olci</operator>
      <sources>
        <sourceProduct>${sourceProduct}</sourceProduct>
        <tomsomiStartProduct>${tomsomiStartProduct}</tomsomiStartProduct>
        <tomsomiEndProduct>${tomsomiEndProduct}</tomsomiEndProduct>
        <ncepStartProduct>${ncepStartProduct}</ncepStartProduct>
        <ncepEndProduct>${ncepEndProduct}</ncepEndProduct>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <validPixelExpression>string</validPixelExpression>
        <salinity>double</salinity>
        <temperature>double</temperature>
        <ozone>double</ozone>
        <press>double</press>
        <TSMfac>double</TSMfac>
        <TSMexp>double</TSMexp>
        <CHLexp>double</CHLexp>
        <CHLfac>double</CHLfac>
        <thresholdRtosaOOS>double</thresholdRtosaOOS>
        <thresholdAcReflecOos>double</thresholdAcReflecOos>
        <thresholdCloudTDown865>double</thresholdCloudTDown865>
        <atmosphericAuxDataPath>string</atmosphericAuxDataPath>
        <alternativeNNPath>string</alternativeNNPath>
        <outputAsRrs>boolean</outputAsRrs>
        <deriveRwFromPathAndTransmittance>boolean</deriveRwFromPathAndTransmittance>
        <useEcmwfAuxData>boolean</useEcmwfAuxData>
        <demName>string</demName>
        <outputRtoa>boolean</outputRtoa>
        <outputRtosaGc>boolean</outputRtosaGc>
        <outputRtosaGcAann>boolean</outputRtosaGcAann>
        <outputRpath>boolean</outputRpath>
        <outputTdown>boolean</outputTdown>
        <outputTup>boolean</outputTup>
        <outputAcReflectance>boolean</outputAcReflectance>
        <outputRhown>boolean</outputRhown>
        <outputOos>boolean</outputOos>
        <outputKd>boolean</outputKd>
        <outputUncertainties>boolean</outputUncertainties>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>
