OPERATOR: c2rcc.seawifs
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt c2rcc.seawifs [options] 

Description:
  Performs atmospheric correction and IOP retrieval on SeaWifs L1C data products.


Source Options:
  -SncepEndProduct=<file>         The second product providing air pressure values for pressure interpolation. Use either the TOMSOMI and NCEP products or the atmosphericAuxdataPath to as source for ozone and air pressure.
                                  This is an optional source.
  -SncepStartProduct=<file>       The first product providing air pressure values for pressure interpolation. Use either the TOMSOMI and NCEP products or the atmosphericAuxdataPath to as source for ozone and air pressure.
                                  This is an optional source.
  -SsourceProduct=<file>          SeaWiFS L1C source product.
                                  This is a mandatory source.
  -StomsomiEndProduct=<file>      The second product providing ozone values for ozone interpolation. Use either the TOMSOMI and NCEP products or the atmosphericAuxdataPath to as source for ozone and air pressure.
                                  This is an optional source.
  -StomsomiStartProduct=<file>    The first product providing ozone values for ozone interpolation. Use either the TOMSOMI and NCEP products or the atmosphericAuxdataPath to as source for ozone and air pressure.
                                  This is an optional source.

Parameter Options:
  -PatmosphericAuxDataPath=<string>    Path to the atmospheric auxiliary data directory. Use either this or tomsomiStartProduct, tomsomiEndProduct, ncepStartProduct and ncepEndProduct to use ozone and air pressure aux data for calculations. If the auxiliary data needed for interpolation not available in this path, the data will automatically downloaded.
  -PdemName=<string>                   The digital elevation model.
                                       Value must be one of 'Copernicus 90m Global DEM', 'Copernicus 30m Global DEM', 'GETASSE30'.
                                       Default value is 'Copernicus 90m Global DEM'.
  -Pelevation=<double>                 Used as fallback if elevation could not be taken from DEM.
                                       Valid interval is (0, 8500).
                                       Default value is '0'.
                                       Parameter unit is 'm'.
  -PoutputAsRrs=<boolean>              Reflectance values in the target product shall be either written as remote sensing or water leaving reflectances
                                       Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputRtosa=<boolean>              Sets parameter 'outputRtosa' to <boolean>.
                                       Default value is 'false'.
  -Pozone=<double>                     The value used as ozone if not provided by auxiliary data
                                       Valid interval is (0, 1000).
                                       Default value is '330'.
                                       Parameter unit is 'DU'.
  -Ppress=<double>                     The surface air pressure at sea level if not provided by auxiliary data
                                       Valid interval is (800, 1040).
                                       Default value is '1000'.
                                       Parameter unit is 'hPa'.
  -Psalinity=<double>                  The value used as salinity for the scene
                                       Valid interval is (0.000028, 43).
                                       Default value is '35.0'.
                                       Parameter unit is 'PSU'.
  -Ptemperature=<double>               The value used as temperature for the scene
                                       Valid interval is (0.000111, 36).
                                       Default value is '15.0'.
                                       Parameter unit is 'C'.
  -PvalidPixelExpression=<string>      Defines the pixels which are valid for processing
                                       Default value is '!(l2_flags.LAND || rhot_865 > 0.25)'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>c2rcc.seawifs</operator>
      <sources>
        <sourceProduct>${sourceProduct}</sourceProduct>
        <tomsomiStartProduct>${tomsomiStartProduct}</tomsomiStartProduct>
        <tomsomiEndProduct>${tomsomiEndProduct}</tomsomiEndProduct>
        <ncepStartProduct>${ncepStartProduct}</ncepStartProduct>
        <ncepEndProduct>${ncepEndProduct}</ncepEndProduct>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <validPixelExpression>string</validPixelExpression>
        <salinity>double</salinity>
        <temperature>double</temperature>
        <ozone>double</ozone>
        <press>double</press>
        <elevation>double</elevation>
        <atmosphericAuxDataPath>string</atmosphericAuxDataPath>
        <outputRtosa>boolean</outputRtosa>

OPERATOR: CiOp
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt CiOp [options] 

Description:
  Colour Index  was developed to differentiate soils in the field. It gives complementary information with the BI and the NDVI.


Source Options:
  -Ssource=<file>    The source product.
                     This is a mandatory source.

Parameter Options:
  -Pdownsampling=<string>       The method used for aggregation (downsampling to a coarser resolution).
                                Value must be one of 'First', 'Min', 'Max', 'Mean', 'Median'.
                                Default value is 'First'.
  -PgreenFactor=<float>         The value of the green source band is multiplied by this value.
                                Default value is '1.0F'.
  -PgreenSourceBand=<string>    The green band for the CI computation. If not provided, the operator will try to find the best fitting band.
  -PredFactor=<float>           The value of the red source band is multiplied by this value.
                                Default value is '1.0F'.
  -PredSourceBand=<string>      The red band for the CI computation. If not provided, the operator will try to find the best fitting band.
  -PresampleType=<string>       If selected band s differ in size, the resample method used before computing the index
                                Value must be one of 'None', 'Lowest resolution', 'Highest resolution'.
                                Default value is 'None'.
  -Pupsampling=<string>         The method used for interpolation (upsampling to a finer resolution).
                                Value must be one of 'Nearest', 'Bilinear', 'Bicubic'.
                                Default value is 'Nearest'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>CiOp</operator>
      <sources>
        <source>${source}</source>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <resampleType>string</resampleType>
        <upsampling>string</upsampling>
        <downsampling>string</downsampling>
        <redFactor>float</redFactor>
        <greenFactor>float</greenFactor>
        <redSourceBand>string</redSourceBand>
        <greenSourceBand>string</greenSourceBand>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

OPERATOR: Coherence
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt Coherence [options] 

Description:
  Estimate coherence from stack of coregistered images


Source Options:
  -SsourceProduct=<file>    Sets source 'sourceProduct' to <filepath>.
                            This is a mandatory source.

Parameter Options:
  -PcohWinAz=<int>                        Size of coherence estimation window in Azimuth direction
                                          Valid interval is (1, 90].
                                          Default value is '10'.
  -PcohWinRg=<int>                        Size of coherence estimation window in Range direction
                                          Valid interval is (1, 90].
                                          Default value is '10'.
  -PdemName=<string>                      The digital elevation model.
                                          Default value is 'SRTM 3Sec'.
  -PexternalDEMApplyEGM=<boolean>         Sets parameter 'externalDEMApplyEGM' to <boolean>.
                                          Default value is 'true'.
  -PexternalDEMFile=<file>                Sets parameter 'externalDEMFile' to <file>.
  -PexternalDEMNoDataValue=<double>       Sets parameter 'externalDEMNoDataValue' to <double>.
                                          Default value is '0'.
  -PorbitDegree=<int>                     Degree of orbit (polynomial) interpolator
                                          Value must be one of '1', '2', '3', '4', '5'.
                                          Default value is '3'.
  -PsingleMaster=<boolean>                Sets parameter 'singleMaster' to <boolean>.
                                          Default value is 'true'.
  -PsquarePixel=<boolean>                 Use ground square pixel
                                          Default value is 'true'.
  -PsrpNumberPoints=<int>                 Number of points for the 'flat earth phase' polynomial estimation
                                          Value must be one of '301', '401', '501', '601', '701', '801', '901', '1001'.
                                          Default value is '501'.
  -PsrpPolynomialDegree=<int>             Order of 'Flat earth phase' polynomial
                                          Value must be one of '1', '2', '3', '4', '5', '6', '7', '8'.
                                          Default value is '5'.
  -PsubtractFlatEarthPhase=<boolean>      Sets parameter 'subtractFlatEarthPhase' to <boolean>.
                                          Default value is 'false'.
  -PsubtractTopographicPhase=<boolean>    Sets parameter 'subtractTopographicPhase' to <boolean>.
                                          Default value is 'false'.
  -PtileExtensionPercent=<string>         Define extension of tile for DEM simulation (optimization parameter).
                                          Default value is '100'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>Coherence</operator>
      <sources>
        <sourceProduct>${sourceProduct}</sourceProduct>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <cohWinAz>int</cohWinAz>
        <cohWinRg>int</cohWinRg>
        <subtractFlatEarthPhase>boolean</subtractFlatEarthPhase>
        <srpPolynomialDegree>int</srpPolynomialDegree>
        <srpNumberPoints>int</srpNumberPoints>
        <orbitDegree>int</orbitDegree>
        <squarePixel>boolean</squarePixel>
        <subtractTopographicPhase>boolean</subtractTopographicPhase>
        <demName>string</demName>
        <externalDEMFile>file</externalDEMFile>
        <externalDEMNoDataValue>double</externalDEMNoDataValue>
        <externalDEMApplyEGM>boolean</externalDEMApplyEGM>
        <tileExtensionPercent>string</tileExtensionPercent>
        <singleMaster>boolean</singleMaster>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

OPERATOR: Collocate
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt Collocate [options] 

Description:
  Collocates two products based on their geo-codings.


Source Options:
  -Sreference=<file>    The source product which serves as reference.
                        This is an optional source.
  -Ssecondary=<file>    The source product which serves as secondary.
                        This is an optional source.

Parameter Options:
  -PcopySecondaryMetadata=<boolean>                  Copies also the metadata of the secondary products to the target.
                                                     Default value is 'false'.
  -PreferenceComponentPattern=<string>               The text pattern to be used when renaming reference components.
                                                     Default value is '${ORIGINAL_NAME}_M'.
  -PreferenceProductName=<string>                    The name of the reference product.
  -PrenameReferenceComponents=<boolean>              Whether or not components of the reference product shall be renamed in the target product.
                                                     Default value is 'true'.
  -PrenameSecondaryComponents=<boolean>              Whether or not components of the secondary product(s) shall be renamed in the target product.
                                                     Default value is 'true'.
  -PresamplingType=<resamplingType>                  The method to be used when resampling the secondary grid onto the reference grid.
                                                     Default value is 'NEAREST_NEIGHBOUR'.
  -PsecondaryComponentPattern=<string>               The text pattern to be used when renaming secondary components.
                                                     Default value is '${ORIGINAL_NAME}_S${SLAVE_NUMBER_ID}'.
  -PsourceProductPaths=<string,string,string,...>    A comma-separated list of file paths specifying the source products
  -PtargetProductType=<string>                       The product type string for the target product (informal)
                                                     Default value is 'COLLOCATED'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>Collocate</operator>
      <sources>
        <reference>${reference}</reference>
        <secondary>${secondary}</secondary>
        <sourceProducts>${sourceProducts}</sourceProducts>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <sourceProductPaths>string,string,string,...</sourceProductPaths>
        <referenceProductName>string</referenceProductName>
        <targetProductType>string</targetProductType>

        <renameReferenceComponents>boolean</renameReferenceComponents>
        <renameSecondaryComponents>boolean</renameSecondaryComponents>
        <referenceComponentPattern>string</referenceComponentPattern>
        <secondaryComponentPattern>string</secondaryComponentPattern>
        <resamplingType>resamplingType</resamplingType>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

OPERATOR: DEM-Assisted-Coregistration
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt DEM-Assisted-Coregistration [options] 

Description:
  Orbit and DEM based co-registration


Parameter Options:
  -PdemName=<string>                         The digital elevation model.
                                             Default value is 'SRTM 3Sec'.
  -PdemResamplingMethod=<string>             Sets parameter 'demResamplingMethod' to <string>.
                                             Default value is 'BICUBIC_INTERPOLATION'.
  -PexternalDEMFile=<file>                   Sets parameter 'externalDEMFile' to <file>.
  -PexternalDEMNoDataValue=<double>          Sets parameter 'externalDEMNoDataValue' to <double>.
                                             Default value is '0'.
  -PmaskOutAreaWithoutElevation=<boolean>    Sets parameter 'maskOutAreaWithoutElevation' to <boolean>.
                                             Default value is 'true'.
  -PoutputRangeAzimuthOffset=<boolean>       Sets parameter 'outputRangeAzimuthOffset' to <boolean>.
                                             Default value is 'false'.
  -PresamplingType=<string>                  The method to be used when resampling the slave grid onto the master grid.
                                             Default value is 'BISINC_5_POINT_INTERPOLATION'.
  -PtileExtensionPercent=<int>               Define tile extension percentage.
                                             Valid interval is [0, *).
                                             Default value is '50'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>DEM-Assisted-Coregistration</operator>
      <sources>
        <sourceProduct>${sourceProduct}</sourceProduct>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <demName>string</demName>
        <demResamplingMethod>string</demResamplingMethod>
        <externalDEMFile>file</externalDEMFile>
        <externalDEMNoDataValue>double</externalDEMNoDataValue>
        <resamplingType>string</resamplingType>
        <tileExtensionPercent>int</tileExtensionPercent>
        <maskOutAreaWithoutElevation>boolean</maskOutAreaWithoutElevation>
        <outputRangeAzimuthOffset>boolean</outputRangeAzimuthOffset>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

==================================================

OPERATOR: Demodulate
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt Demodulate [options] 

Description:
  Demodulation and deramping of SLC data


Source Options:
  -SsourceProduct=<file>    Sets source 'sourceProduct' to <filepath>.
                            This is a mandatory source.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>Demodulate</operator>
      <sources>
        <sourceProduct>${sourceProduct}</sourceProduct>
      </sources>
      <parameters/>
    </node>
  </graph>

OPERATOR: Double-Difference-Interferogram
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt Double-Difference-Interferogram [options] 

Description:
  Compute double difference interferogram


Source Options:
  -Ssource=<file>    Sets source 'source' to <filepath>.
                     This is a mandatory source.

Parameter Options:
  -PcohWinSize=<string>          Sets parameter 'cohWinSize' to <string>.
                                 Value must be one of '3', '5', '9', '11'.
                                 Default value is '5'.
  -PoutputCoherence=<boolean>    Output coherence for overlapped area
                                 Default value is 'false'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>Double-Difference-Interferogram</operator>
      <sources>
        <source>${source}</source>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <outputCoherence>boolean</outputCoherence>
        <cohWinSize>string</cohWinSize>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

==================================================

OPERATOR: DviOp
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt DviOp [options] 

Description:
  Difference Vegetation Index retrieves the Isovegetation lines parallel to soil line


Source Options:
  -Ssource=<file>    The source product.
                     This is a mandatory source.

Parameter Options:
  -Pdownsampling=<string>     The method used for aggregation (downsampling to a coarser resolution).
                              Value must be one of 'First', 'Min', 'Max', 'Mean', 'Median'.
                              Default value is 'First'.
  -PnirFactor=<float>         The value of the NIR source band is multiplied by this value.
                              Default value is '1.0F'.
  -PnirSourceBand=<string>    The near-infrared band for the DVI computation. If not provided, the operator will try to find the best fitting band.
  -PredFactor=<float>         The value of the red source band is multiplied by this value.
                              Default value is '1.0F'.
  -PredSourceBand=<string>    The red band for the DVI computation. If not provided, the operator will try to find the best fitting band.
  -PresampleType=<string>     If selected band s differ in size, the resample method used before computing the index
                              Value must be one of 'None', 'Lowest resolution', 'Highest resolution'.
                              Default value is 'None'.
  -Pupsampling=<string>       The method used for interpolation (upsampling to a finer resolution).
                              Value must be one of 'Nearest', 'Bilinear', 'Bicubic'.
                              Default value is 'Nearest'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>DviOp</operator>
      <sources>
        <source>${source}</source>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <resampleType>string</resampleType>
        <upsampling>string</upsampling>
        <downsampling>string</downsampling>
        <redFactor>float</redFactor>
        <nirFactor>float</nirFactor>
        <redSourceBand>string</redSourceBand>
        <nirSourceBand>string</nirSourceBand>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

==================================================

----------------------------------------

  gpt EAP-Phase-Correction [options]

  EAP Phase Correction

        <source>${source}</source>

OPERATOR: EcostressSwath2GridOp
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt EcostressSwath2GridOp [options] 

Description:
  Performs ECOSTRESS Swath to Grid conversion to a specified CRS and radiance to brightness temperature conversion, using the algorithm from 'ECOSTRESS Swath to Grid Conversion Script' by LP DAAC (https://git.earthdata.nasa.gov/projects/LPDUR/repos/ecostress_swath2grid/).


Source Options:
  -SecoProduct=<file>    The source product to be converted from Swath to Grid.
                         Valid product types must match 'ECOSTRESS-.*'.
                         This is a mandatory source.
  -SgeoProduct=<file>    The source GEO product from which the geocoding will be extracted.
                         Valid product types must match 'ECOSTRESS-L1B-GEO'.
                         This is a mandatory source.

Parameter Options:
  -PcrsIN=<string>      The projection desired for the output.
                        Value must be one of 'GEO', 'UTM'.
                        Default value is 'GEO'.
  -Pr2b=<boolean>       The optional argument to convert radiance to brightness temperature for the L1B products
                        Default value is 'false'.
  -PutmZone=<string>    The UTM zone (EPSG Code) desired for all outputs - only required if needed to override default UTM zone which is assigned based on the center location for each ECOSTRESS granule.
                        Default value is 'auto_lookup'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>EcostressSwath2GridOp</operator>
      <sources>
        <ecoProduct>${ecoProduct}</ecoProduct>
        <geoProduct>${geoProduct}</geoProduct>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <crsIN>string</crsIN>
        <utmZone>string</utmZone>
        <r2b>boolean</r2b>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

OPERATOR: Ellipsoid-Correction-RD
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt Ellipsoid-Correction-RD [options] 

Description:
  Ellipsoid correction with RD method and average scene height


Source Options:
  -Ssource=<file>    Sets source 'source' to <filepath>.
                     This is a mandatory source.

Parameter Options:
  -PalignToStandardGrid=<boolean>                 Force the image grid to be aligned with a specific point
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PapplyRadiometricNormalization=<boolean>       Sets parameter 'applyRadiometricNormalization' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PauxFile=<string>                              The auxiliary file
                                                  Value must be one of 'Latest Auxiliary File', 'Product Auxiliary File', 'External Auxiliary File'.

  -PdemName=<string>                              The digital elevation model.
                                                  Default value is 'SRTM 3Sec'.
  -PdemResamplingMethod=<string>                  Sets parameter 'demResamplingMethod' to <string>.
                                                  Value must be one of 'NEAREST_NEIGHBOUR', 'BILINEAR_INTERPOLATION', 'CUBIC_CONVOLUTION', 'BISINC_5_POINT_INTERPOLATION', 'BISINC_11_POINT_INTERPOLATION', 'BISINC_21_POINT_INTERPOLATION', 'BICUBIC_INTERPOLATION', 'DELAUNAY_INTERPOLATION'.
                                                  Default value is 'BILINEAR_INTERPOLATION'.
  -PexternalAuxFile=<file>                        The antenne elevation pattern gain auxiliary data file.
  -PexternalDEMApplyEGM=<boolean>                 Sets parameter 'externalDEMApplyEGM' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'true'.
  -PexternalDEMFile=<file>                        Sets parameter 'externalDEMFile' to <file>.
  -PexternalDEMNoDataValue=<double>               Sets parameter 'externalDEMNoDataValue' to <double>.
                                                  Default value is '0'.
  -PimgResamplingMethod=<string>                  Sets parameter 'imgResamplingMethod' to <string>.
                                                  Value must be one of 'NEAREST_NEIGHBOUR', 'BILINEAR_INTERPOLATION', 'CUBIC_CONVOLUTION', 'BISINC_5_POINT_INTERPOLATION', 'BISINC_11_POINT_INTERPOLATION', 'BISINC_21_POINT_INTERPOLATION', 'BICUBIC_INTERPOLATION'.
                                                  Default value is 'BILINEAR_INTERPOLATION'.
  -PincidenceAngleForGamma0=<string>              Sets parameter 'incidenceAngleForGamma0' to <string>.
                                                  Value must be one of 'Use incidence angle from Ellipsoid', 'Use local incidence angle from DEM', 'Use projected local incidence angle from DEM'.
                                                  Default value is 'Use projected local incidence angle from DEM'.
  -PincidenceAngleForSigma0=<string>              Sets parameter 'incidenceAngleForSigma0' to <string>.
                                                  Value must be one of 'Use incidence angle from Ellipsoid', 'Use local incidence angle from DEM', 'Use projected local incidence angle from DEM'.
                                                  Default value is 'Use projected local incidence angle from DEM'.
  -PmapProjection=<string>                        The coordinate reference system in well known text format
                                                  Default value is 'WGS84(DD)'.
  -PnodataValueAtSea=<boolean>                    Mask the sea with no data value (faster)
                                                  Default value is 'true'.
  -PoutputComplex=<boolean>                       Sets parameter 'outputComplex' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PpixelSpacingInDegree=<double>                 The pixel spacing in degrees
                                                  Default value is '0'.
  -PpixelSpacingInMeter=<double>                  The pixel spacing in meters
                                                  Default value is '0'.
  -PsaveBetaNought=<boolean>                      Sets parameter 'saveBetaNought' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PsaveDEM=<boolean>                             Sets parameter 'saveDEM' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PsaveGammaNought=<boolean>                     Sets parameter 'saveGammaNought' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PsaveIncidenceAngleFromEllipsoid=<boolean>     Sets parameter 'saveIncidenceAngleFromEllipsoid' to <boolean>.

  -PsaveLatLon=<boolean>                          Sets parameter 'saveLatLon' to <boolean>.

  -PsaveSelectedSourceBand=<boolean>              Sets parameter 'saveSelectedSourceBand' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'true'.
  -PsaveSigmaNought=<boolean>                     Sets parameter 'saveSigmaNought' to <boolean>.
                                                  Default value is 'false'.
  -PsourceBands=<string,string,string,...>        The list of source bands.
  -PstandardGridOriginX=<double>                  x-coordinate of the standard grid's origin point

OPERATOR: Enhanced-Spectral-Diversity
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt Enhanced-Spectral-Diversity [options] 

Description:
  Estimate constant range and azimuth offsets for a stack of images


Source Options:
  -Ssource=<file>    Sets source 'source' to <filepath>.
                     This is a mandatory source.

Parameter Options:
  -PcohThreshold=<double>                The coherence threshold for outlier removal
                                         Valid interval is (0, 1].
                                         Default value is '0.3'.
  -PdoNotWriteTargetBands=<boolean>      Do not write target bands
                                         Default value is 'false'.
  -PesdEstimator=<string>                ESD estimator used for azimuth shift computation
                                         Value must be one of 'Average', 'Periodogram'.
                                         Default value is 'Periodogram'.
  -PfineWinAccAzimuth=<string>           Sets parameter 'fineWinAccAzimuth' to <string>.
                                         Value must be one of '2', '4', '8', '16', '32', '64'.
                                         Default value is '16'.
  -PfineWinAccRange=<string>             Sets parameter 'fineWinAccRange' to <string>.
                                         Value must be one of '2', '4', '8', '16', '32', '64'.
                                         Default value is '16'.
  -PfineWinHeightStr=<string>            Sets parameter 'fineWinHeightStr' to <string>.
                                         Value must be one of '32', '64', '128', '256', '512', '1024', '2048'.
                                         Default value is '512'.
  -PfineWinOversampling=<string>         Sets parameter 'fineWinOversampling' to <string>.
                                         Value must be one of '32', '64', '128', '256'.
                                         Default value is '128'.
  -PfineWinWidthStr=<string>             Sets parameter 'fineWinWidthStr' to <string>.
                                         Value must be one of '32', '64', '128', '256', '512', '1024', '2048'.
                                         Default value is '512'.
  -PintegrationMethod=<string>           Method used for integrating the shifts network.
                                         Value must be one of 'L1', 'L2', 'L1 and L2'.
                                         Default value is 'L1 and L2'.
  -PmaxTemporalBaseline=<int>            Maximum temporal baseline (in days or number of images depending on the Temporal baseline type) between pairs of images to construct the network. Any number < 1 will generate a network with all of the possible pairs.
                                         Default value is '4'.
  -PnumBlocksPerOverlap=<int>            The number of windows per overlap for ESD
                                         Valid interval is [1, 20].
                                         Default value is '10'.
  -PoverallAzimuthShift=<double>         The overall azimuth shift
                                         Default value is '0.0'.
  -PoverallRangeShift=<double>           The overall range shift
                                         Default value is '0.0'.
  -PtemporalBaselineType=<string>        Baseline type for building the integration network
                                         Value must be one of 'Number of images', 'Number of days'.
                                         Default value is 'Number of images'.
  -PuseSuppliedAzimuthShift=<boolean>    Use user supplied azimuth shift
                                         Default value is 'false'.
  -PuseSuppliedRangeShift=<boolean>      Use user supplied range shift
                                         Default value is 'false'.
  -PweightFunc=<string>                  Weight function of the coherence to use for azimuth shift estimation
                                         Value must be one of 'None', 'Linear', 'Quadratic', 'Inv Quadratic'.
                                         Default value is 'Inv Quadratic'.
  -PxCorrThreshold=<double>              The peak cross-correlation threshold
                                         Valid interval is (0, *).
                                         Default value is '0.1'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>Enhanced-Spectral-Diversity</operator>
      <sources>
        <source>${source}</source>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <fineWinWidthStr>string</fineWinWidthStr>
        <fineWinHeightStr>string</fineWinHeightStr>
        <fineWinAccAzimuth>string</fineWinAccAzimuth>
        <fineWinAccRange>string</fineWinAccRange>
        <fineWinOversampling>string</fineWinOversampling>
        <xCorrThreshold>double</xCorrThreshold>
        <cohThreshold>double</cohThreshold>
        <numBlocksPerOverlap>int</numBlocksPerOverlap>
        <esdEstimator>string</esdEstimator>
        <weightFunc>string</weightFunc>
        <temporalBaselineType>string</temporalBaselineType>
        <maxTemporalBaseline>int</maxTemporalBaseline>
        <integrationMethod>string</integrationMethod>
        <doNotWriteTargetBands>boolean</doNotWriteTargetBands>
        <useSuppliedRangeShift>boolean</useSuppliedRangeShift>
        <overallRangeShift>double</overallRangeShift>
        <useSuppliedAzimuthShift>boolean</useSuppliedAzimuthShift>
        <overallAzimuthShift>double</overallAzimuthShift>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

----------------------------------------

  gpt ForestCoverChangeOp [options]

  Creates forest change masks out of two source products


Source Options:

                              This is a mandatory source.
  -SrecentProduct=<file>      The source product to be modified.
                              This is a mandatory source.

Parameter Options:
  -PcurrentProductSourceMaskFile=<file>           A binary raster file to be added as mask to the output product
  -PdegreesOfFreedom=<double>                     Degrees of freedom used for the Chi distribution trimming process
                                                  Default value is '3.3'.
  -PforestCoverPercentage=<float>                 Specifies the percentage of forest cover per segment
                                                  Default value is '95.0'.

                                                  Default value is '40, 50, 60, 61, 62, 70, 71, 72, 80, 81, 82, 90, 100, 110, 160, 170'.
  -PlandCoverName=<string>                        Sets parameter 'landCoverName' to <string>.
                                                  Default value is 'CCILandCover-2015'.
  -PmergingCostCriterion=<string>                 The method to compute the region merging.
                                                  Value must be one of 'Spring', 'Baatz & Schape', 'Full Lamda Schedule'.
                                                  Default value is 'Spring'.
  -PpreviousProductSourceMaskFile=<file>          A binary raster file to be added as mask to the output product
  -PregionMergingCriterion=<string>               The method to check the region merging.
                                                  Value must be one of 'Best Fitting', 'Local Mutual Best Fitting'.

  -PshapeWeight=<float>                           The shape weight.
                                                  Default value is '0.5'.
  -PspectralWeight=<float>                        The spectral weight.
                                                  Default value is '0.5'.
  -Pthreshold=<float>                             The threshold.
                                                  Default value is '5.0'.
  -PtotalIterationsForSecondSegmentation=<int>    The total number of iterations.
                                                  Default value is '10'.

Graph XML Format:

  -PincludeIntermediateResults=<boolean>      Whether or not the intermediate results shall be written to the target output
                                              Default value is 'true'.
  -PinputIsIrradianceReflectance=<boolean>    If enabled, the source reflectances will be converted to radiance reflectances by dividing it by PI before passing to the algorithm.
                                              Default value is 'false'.
  -Pinstrument=<instrument>                   The instrument to compute FU for.
                                              Default value is 'AUTO_DETECT'.
  -PreflectanceNamePattern=<string>           The used reflectance band names must match the given pattern. Useful, if there is more then one spectrum in the product.
  -PvalidExpression=<string>                  An expression to filter which pixel are considered.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>FuClassification</operator>
      <sources>
        <source>${source}</source>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <copyAllSourceBands>boolean</copyAllSourceBands>
        <inputIsIrradianceReflectance>boolean</inputIsIrradianceReflectance>
        <validExpression>string</validExpression>
        <reflectanceNamePattern>string</reflectanceNamePattern>
        <instrument>instrument</instrument>
        <includeDominantLambda>boolean</includeDominantLambda>
        <includeIntermediateResults>boolean</includeIntermediateResults>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt GemiOp [options] 

Description:
  This retrieves the Global Environmental Monitoring Index (GEMI).


Source Options:
  -Ssource=<file>    The source product.
                     This is a mandatory source.

Parameter Options:
  -Pdownsampling=<string>     The method used for aggregation (downsampling to a coarser resolution).
                              Value must be one of 'First', 'Min', 'Max', 'Mean', 'Median'.
                              Default value is 'First'.
  -PnirFactor=<float>         The value of the NIR source band is multiplied by this value.
                              Default value is '1.0F'.
  -PnirSourceBand=<string>    The near-infrared band for the GEMI computation. If not provided, the operator will try to find the best fitting band.
  -PredFactor=<float>         The value of the RED source band is multiplied by this value.
                              Default value is '1.0F'.
  -PredSourceBand=<string>    The red band for the GEMI computation. If not provided, the operator will try to find the best fitting band.
  -PresampleType=<string>     If selected band s differ in size, the resample method used before computing the index
                              Value must be one of 'None', 'Lowest resolution', 'Highest resolution'.
                              Default value is 'None'.
  -Pupsampling=<string>       The method used for interpolation (upsampling to a finer resolution).
                              Value must be one of 'Nearest', 'Bilinear', 'Bicubic'.
                              Default value is 'Nearest'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">

      <sources>
        <source>${source}</source>
      </sources>

        <nirFactor>float</nirFactor>

OPERATOR: Interferogram
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt Interferogram [options] 

Description:
  Compute interferograms from stack of coregistered S-1 images


Source Options:
  -SsourceProduct=<file>    Sets source 'sourceProduct' to <filepath>.
                            This is a mandatory source.

Parameter Options:
  -PcohWinAz=<int>                        Size of coherence estimation window in Azimuth direction
                                          Default value is '10'.
  -PcohWinRg=<int>                        Size of coherence estimation window in Range direction
                                          Default value is '10'.
  -PdemName=<string>                      The digital elevation model.
                                          Default value is 'SRTM 3Sec'.
  -PexternalDEMApplyEGM=<boolean>         Sets parameter 'externalDEMApplyEGM' to <boolean>.
                                          Default value is 'true'.
  -PexternalDEMFile=<file>                Sets parameter 'externalDEMFile' to <file>.
  -PexternalDEMNoDataValue=<double>       Sets parameter 'externalDEMNoDataValue' to <double>.
                                          Default value is '0'.
  -PincludeCoherence=<boolean>            Sets parameter 'includeCoherence' to <boolean>.
                                          Default value is 'true'.
  -PorbitDegree=<int>                     Degree of orbit (polynomial) interpolator
                                          Value must be one of '1', '2', '3', '4', '5'.
                                          Default value is '3'.
  -PoutputElevation=<boolean>             Sets parameter 'outputElevation' to <boolean>.
                                          Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputFlatEarthPhase=<boolean>        Sets parameter 'outputFlatEarthPhase' to <boolean>.
                                          Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputLatLon=<boolean>                Sets parameter 'outputLatLon' to <boolean>.
                                          Default value is 'false'.
  -PoutputTopoPhase=<boolean>             Sets parameter 'outputTopoPhase' to <boolean>.
                                          Default value is 'false'.
  -PsquarePixel=<boolean>                 Use ground square pixel
                                          Default value is 'true'.
  -PsrpNumberPoints=<int>                 Number of points for the 'flat earth phase' polynomial estimation
                                          Value must be one of '301', '401', '501', '601', '701', '801', '901', '1001'.
                                          Default value is '501'.
  -PsrpPolynomialDegree=<int>             Order of 'Flat earth phase' polynomial
                                          Value must be one of '1', '2', '3', '4', '5', '6', '7', '8'.
                                          Default value is '5'.
  -PsubtractFlatEarthPhase=<boolean>      Sets parameter 'subtractFlatEarthPhase' to <boolean>.
                                          Default value is 'true'.
  -PsubtractTopographicPhase=<boolean>    Sets parameter 'subtractTopographicPhase' to <boolean>.
                                          Default value is 'false'.
  -PtileExtensionPercent=<string>         Define extension of tile for DEM simulation (optimization parameter).
                                          Default value is '100'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>Interferogram</operator>
      <sources>
        <sourceProduct>${sourceProduct}</sourceProduct>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <subtractFlatEarthPhase>boolean</subtractFlatEarthPhase>
        <srpPolynomialDegree>int</srpPolynomialDegree>
        <srpNumberPoints>int</srpNumberPoints>
        <orbitDegree>int</orbitDegree>
        <includeCoherence>boolean</includeCoherence>
        <cohWinAz>int</cohWinAz>
        <cohWinRg>int</cohWinRg>
        <squarePixel>boolean</squarePixel>
        <subtractTopographicPhase>boolean</subtractTopographicPhase>
        <demName>string</demName>
        <externalDEMFile>file</externalDEMFile>
        <externalDEMNoDataValue>double</externalDEMNoDataValue>
        <externalDEMApplyEGM>boolean</externalDEMApplyEGM>
        <tileExtensionPercent>string</tileExtensionPercent>
        <outputFlatEarthPhase>boolean</outputFlatEarthPhase>
        <outputTopoPhase>boolean</outputTopoPhase>

                                   Valid interval is [0, 1].
                                   Default value is '0.2'.
  -Psigma=<int>                    Standard deviation for Gaussian filter
                                   Default value is '81'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>IonosphericCorrection</operator>
      <sources>
        <sourceProduct>${sourceProduct}</sourceProduct>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <sigma>int</sigma>
        <coherenceThreshold>double</coherenceThreshold>
        <minCoherence>double</minCoherence>
      </parameters>
    </node>

                              Default value is '1.0F'.

  -PresampleType=<string>     If selected band s differ in size, the resample method used before computing the index
                              Value must be one of 'None', 'Lowest resolution', 'Highest resolution'.
                              Default value is 'None'.
  -Pupsampling=<string>       The method used for interpolation (upsampling to a finer resolution).
                              Value must be one of 'Nearest', 'Bilinear', 'Bicubic'.
                              Default value is 'Nearest'.

OPERATOR: Merge
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt Merge [options] 

Description:
  Allows merging of several source products by using specified 'master' as reference product.


Source Options:
  -SmasterProduct=<file>    The master, which serves as the reference, e.g. providing the geo-information.
                            This is a mandatory source.

Parameter Options:
  -PgeographicError=<float>    Defines the maximum lat/lon error in degree between the products. If set to NaN no check for compatible geographic boundary is performed
                               Default value is '1.0E-5f'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>Merge</operator>
      <sources>
        <masterProduct>${masterProduct}</masterProduct>
        <sourceProducts>${sourceProducts}</sourceProducts>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <includes>
          <include>
            <productId>string</productId>
            <name>string</name>
            <newName>string</newName>
            <namePattern>string</namePattern>
          </include>
          <_.002e../>
        </includes>
        <excludes>
          <exclude>
            <productId>string</productId>
            <name>string</name>
            <newName>string</newName>
            <namePattern>string</namePattern>
          </exclude>
          <_.002e../>
        </excludes>
        <geographicError>float</geographicError>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

OPERATOR: Meris.CorrectRadiometry
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt Meris.CorrectRadiometry [options] 

Description:
  Performs radiometric corrections on MERIS L1b data products.


Source Options:
  -Ssource=<file>    The source product.
                     This is a mandatory source.

Parameter Options:
  -PdoCalibration=<boolean>               Whether to perform the calibration.
                                          Default value is 'true'.
  -PdoEqualization=<boolean>              Perform removal of detector-to-detector systematic radiometric differences in MERIS L1b data products.
                                          Default value is 'true'.
  -PdoRadToRefl=<boolean>                 Whether to perform radiance-to-reflectance conversion. When selecting ENVISAT as target format, the radiance to reflectance conversion can not be performed.
                                          Default value is 'false'.
  -PdoSmile=<boolean>                     Whether to perform Smile-effect correction.
                                          Default value is 'true'.
  -PreproVersion=<reprocessingVersion>    The version of the reprocessing the product comes from. Is only used if equalisation is enabled.
                                          Value must be one of 'AUTO_DETECT', 'REPROCESSING_2', 'REPROCESSING_3'.
                                          Default value is 'AUTO_DETECT'.
  -PsourceRacFile=<file>                  The radiometric correction auxiliary file for the source product. The default 'MER_RAC_AXVIEC20050708_135553_20021224_121445_20041213_220000'
  -PtargetRacFile=<file>                  The radiometric correction auxiliary file for the target product. The default 'MER_RAC_AXVACR20091016_154511_20021224_121445_20041213_220000'

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>Meris.CorrectRadiometry</operator>
      <sources>
        <source>${source}</source>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <doCalibration>boolean</doCalibration>
        <sourceRacFile>file</sourceRacFile>
        <targetRacFile>file</targetRacFile>
        <doSmile>boolean</doSmile>
        <doEqualization>boolean</doEqualization>
        <reproVersion>reprocessingVersion</reproVersion>
        <doRadToRefl>boolean</doRadToRefl>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

                                Default value is 'First'.

  -PmirFactor=<float>           The value of the MIR source band is multiplied by this value.
                                Default value is '1.0F'.
  -PmirSourceBand=<string>      The mid-infrared band for the MNDWI computation. If not provided, the operator will try to find the best fitting band.
  -PresampleType=<string>       If selected band s differ in size, the resample method used before computing the index
                                Value must be one of 'None', 'Lowest resolution', 'Highest resolution'.
                                Default value is 'None'.
  -Pupsampling=<string>         The method used for interpolation (upsampling to a finer resolution).
                                Value must be one of 'Nearest', 'Bilinear', 'Bicubic'.
                                Default value is 'Nearest'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">

      <sources>

      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <resampleType>string</resampleType>
        <upsampling>string</upsampling>
        <downsampling>string</downsampling>
        <greenFactor>float</greenFactor>
        <mirFactor>float</mirFactor>
        <greenSourceBand>string</greenSourceBand>
        <mirSourceBand>string</mirSourceBand>
      </parameters>

OPERATOR: Mosaic
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt Mosaic [options] <source-file-1> <source-file-2> ...

Description:
  Creates a mosaic out of a set of source products.


Source Options:
  -SupdateProduct=<file>    A product to be updated.
                            This is an optional source.

Parameter Options:
  -Pcombine=<string>               Specifies the way how conditions are combined.
                                   Value must be one of 'OR', 'AND'.
                                   Default value is 'OR'.
  -Pcrs=<string>                   The CRS of the target product, represented as WKT or authority code.
                                   Default value is 'EPSG:4326'.
  -PeastBound=<double>             The eastern longitude.
                                   Valid interval is [-180,180].
                                   Default value is '30.0'.
  -PelevationModelName=<string>    The name of the elevation model for the orthorectification.
  -PnorthBound=<double>            The northern latitude.
                                   Valid interval is [-90,90].
                                   Default value is '75.0'.
  -Porthorectify=<boolean>         Whether the source product should be orthorectified.
                                   Default value is 'false'.
  -PpixelSizeX=<double>            Size of a pixel in X-direction in map units.
                                   Default value is '0.05'.
  -PpixelSizeY=<double>            Size of a pixel in Y-direction in map units.
                                   Default value is '0.05'.
  -Presampling=<string>            The method used for resampling.
                                   Value must be one of 'Nearest', 'Bilinear', 'Bicubic'.
                                   Default value is 'Nearest'.
  -PsouthBound=<double>            The southern latitude.
                                   Valid interval is [-90,90].
                                   Default value is '35.0'.
  -PwestBound=<double>             The western longitude.
                                   Valid interval is [-180,180].
                                   Default value is '-15.0'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>Mosaic</operator>
      <sources>
        <updateProduct>${updateProduct}</updateProduct>
        <sourceProducts>${sourceProducts}</sourceProducts>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <variables>
          <variable>
            <name>string</name>
            <expression>string</expression>
          </variable>
          <_.002e../>
        </variables>
        <conditions>
          <condition>
            <name>string</name>
            <expression>string</expression>
            <output>boolean</output>
          </condition>
          <_.002e../>
        </conditions>
        <combine>string</combine>
        <crs>string</crs>
        <orthorectify>boolean</orthorectify>
        <elevationModelName>string</elevationModelName>
        <resampling>string</resampling>
        <westBound>double</westBound>
        <northBound>double</northBound>
        <eastBound>double</eastBound>
        <southBound>double</southBound>
        <pixelSizeX>double</pixelSizeX>
        <pixelSizeY>double</pixelSizeY>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

                                                      Default value is '0.005'.
  -Presampling=<string>                               The method used for resampling.
                                                      Value must be one of 'Nearest', 'Bilinear', 'Bicubic'.
                                                      Default value is 'Nearest'.
  -PsouthBound=<double>                               The southern latitude.
                                                      Valid interval is [-90,90].
                                                      Default value is '0'.
  -Pvariables=<variable,variable,variable,...>        Specifies the bands in the target product.
  -PwestBound=<double>                                The western longitude.

OPERATOR: Multi-Temporal-Speckle-Filter
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt Multi-Temporal-Speckle-Filter [options] 

Description:
  Speckle Reduction using Multitemporal Filtering


Source Options:
  -Ssource=<file>    Sets source 'source' to <filepath>.
                     This is a mandatory source.

Parameter Options:
  -PanSize=<int>                              The Adaptive Neighbourhood size
                                              Valid interval is (1, 200].
                                              Default value is '50'.
  -PdampingFactor=<int>                       The damping factor (Frost filter only)
                                              Valid interval is (0, 100].
                                              Default value is '2'.
  -Penl=<double>                              The number of looks
                                              Valid interval is (0, *).
                                              Default value is '1.0'.
  -PestimateENL=<boolean>                     Sets parameter 'estimateENL' to <boolean>.
                                              Default value is 'false'.
  -Pfilter=<string>                           Sets parameter 'filter' to <string>.
                                              Value must be one of 'None', 'Boxcar', 'Median', 'Frost', 'Gamma Map', 'Lee', 'Refined Lee', 'Lee Sigma', 'IDAN'.
                                              Default value is 'Lee Sigma'.
  -PfilterSizeX=<int>                         The kernel x dimension
                                              Valid interval is (1, 100].
                                              Default value is '3'.
  -PfilterSizeY=<int>                         The kernel y dimension
                                              Valid interval is (1, 100].
                                              Default value is '3'.
  -PnumLooksStr=<string>                      Sets parameter 'numLooksStr' to <string>.
                                              Value must be one of '1', '2', '3', '4'.
                                              Default value is '1'.
  -PsigmaStr=<string>                         Sets parameter 'sigmaStr' to <string>.
                                              Value must be one of '0.5', '0.6', '0.7', '0.8', '0.9'.
                                              Default value is '0.9'.
  -PsourceBands=<string,string,string,...>    The list of source bands.
  -PtargetWindowSizeStr=<string>              Sets parameter 'targetWindowSizeStr' to <string>.
                                              Value must be one of '3x3', '5x5'.
                                              Default value is '3x3'.
  -PwindowSize=<string>                       Sets parameter 'windowSize' to <string>.
                                              Value must be one of '5x5', '7x7', '9x9', '11x11', '13x13', '15x15', '17x17'.
                                              Default value is '7x7'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>Multi-Temporal-Speckle-Filter</operator>
      <sources>
        <source>${source}</source>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <sourceBands>string,string,string,...</sourceBands>
        <filter>string</filter>
        <filterSizeX>int</filterSizeX>
        <filterSizeY>int</filterSizeY>
        <dampingFactor>int</dampingFactor>

OPERATOR: Ndi45Op
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt Ndi45Op [options] 

Description:
  Normalized Difference Index using bands 4 and 5


Source Options:
  -Ssource=<file>    The source product.
                     This is a mandatory source.

Parameter Options:
  -Pdownsampling=<string>      The method used for aggregation (downsampling to a coarser resolution).
                               Value must be one of 'First', 'Min', 'Max', 'Mean', 'Median'.
                               Default value is 'First'.
  -PredB4Factor=<float>        The value of the red source band (B4) is multiplied by this value.
                               Default value is '1.0F'.
  -PredB5Factor=<float>        The value of the red source band (B5) is multiplied by this value.
                               Default value is '1.0F'.
  -PredSourceBand4=<string>    The red band (B4) for the NDI45 computation. If not provided, the operator will try to find the best fitting band.
  -PredSourceBand5=<string>    The red band (B5) for the NDI45 computation. If not provided, the operator will try to find the best fitting band.
  -PresampleType=<string>      If selected band s differ in size, the resample method used before computing the index
                               Value must be one of 'None', 'Lowest resolution', 'Highest resolution'.
                               Default value is 'None'.
  -Pupsampling=<string>        The method used for interpolation (upsampling to a finer resolution).
                               Value must be one of 'Nearest', 'Bilinear', 'Bicubic'.
                               Default value is 'Nearest'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>Ndi45Op</operator>
      <sources>
        <source>${source}</source>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <resampleType>string</resampleType>
        <upsampling>string</upsampling>
        <downsampling>string</downsampling>
        <redB4Factor>float</redB4Factor>
        <redB5Factor>float</redB5Factor>
        <redSourceBand4>string</redSourceBand4>
        <redSourceBand5>string</redSourceBand5>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

OPERATOR: Offset-Tracking
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt Offset-Tracking [options] 

Description:
  Create velocity vectors from offset tracking


Source Options:
  -SsourceProduct=<file>    Sets source 'sourceProduct' to <filepath>.
                            This is a mandatory source.

Parameter Options:
  -PaverageBoxSize=<string>              Sets parameter 'averageBoxSize' to <string>.
                                         Value must be one of '3', '5', '9', '11'.
                                         Default value is '5'.
  -PfillHoles=<boolean>                  Sets parameter 'fillHoles' to <boolean>.
                                         Default value is 'true'.
  -PgridAzimuthSpacing=<int>             The output grid azimuth spacing in pixels
                                         Valid interval is (1, *).
                                         Default value is '40'.
  -PgridRangeSpacing=<int>               The output grid range spacing in pixels
                                         Valid interval is (1, *).
                                         Default value is '40'.
  -PmaxVelocity=<double>                 The threshold for eliminating invalid GCPs
                                         Valid interval is (0, *).
                                         Default value is '5.0'.
  -Pradius=<int>                         Radius for Hole-Filling
                                         Valid interval is (0, *).
                                         Default value is '4'.
  -PregistrationOversampling=<string>    Sets parameter 'registrationOversampling' to <string>.
                                         Value must be one of '2', '4', '8', '16', '32', '64', '128', '256', '512'.
                                         Default value is '16'.
  -PregistrationWindowHeight=<string>    Sets parameter 'registrationWindowHeight' to <string>.
                                         Value must be one of '32', '64', '128', '256', '512', '1024', '2048'.
                                         Default value is '128'.
  -PregistrationWindowWidth=<string>     Sets parameter 'registrationWindowWidth' to <string>.
                                         Value must be one of '32', '64', '128', '256', '512', '1024', '2048'.
                                         Default value is '128'.
  -PresamplingType=<string>              Methods for velocity interpolation.
                                         Value must be one of 'NEAREST_NEIGHBOUR', 'BILINEAR_INTERPOLATION', 'BICUBIC_INTERPOLATION', 'BISINC_5_POINT_INTERPOLATION', 'CUBIC_CONVOLUTION'.
                                         Default value is 'BICUBIC_INTERPOLATION'.
  -ProiVector=<string>                   Sets parameter 'roiVector' to <string>.
  -PspatialAverage=<boolean>             Sets parameter 'spatialAverage' to <boolean>.
                                         Default value is 'true'.
  -PxCorrThreshold=<double>              The cross-correlation threshold
                                         Valid interval is (0, *).
                                         Default value is '0.1'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">

      <sources>
        <sourceProduct>${sourceProduct}</sourceProduct>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <gridAzimuthSpacing>int</gridAzimuthSpacing>
        <gridRangeSpacing>int</gridRangeSpacing>
        <registrationWindowWidth>string</registrationWindowWidth>
        <registrationWindowHeight>string</registrationWindowHeight>
        <xCorrThreshold>double</xCorrThreshold>
        <registrationOversampling>string</registrationOversampling>
        <averageBoxSize>string</averageBoxSize>
        <maxVelocity>double</maxVelocity>
        <radius>int</radius>
        <resamplingType>string</resamplingType>
        <spatialAverage>boolean</spatialAverage>
        <fillHoles>boolean</fillHoles>
        <roiVector>string</roiVector>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

OPERATOR: OlciSensorHarmonisation
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt OlciSensorHarmonisation [options] 

Description:
  Performs sensor harmonisation on OLCI L1b product. Implements algorithm described in 'OLCI A/B Tandem Phase Analysis'


Source Options:
  -Sl1bProduct=<file>    OLCI L1b or fully compatible product.
                         This is a mandatory source.

Parameter Options:
  -PcopyInputBands=<boolean>                   If set to true, all bands of the input product (except for the radiances) are copied to the target product. If set to false, only the tie-point rasters are copied
                                               Default value is 'false'.
  -PperformSensorCrossCalibration=<boolean>    If set to true, in addition to the camera homogenisation, sensor cross-calibration (i.e. S3A->S3B or S3B->S3A) is performed using linear regression
                                               Default value is 'false'.

Description:
  Stitches multiple SLSTR L1B product dissemination units (PDUs) of the same orbit to a single product.


Parameter Options:
  -PsourceProductPaths=<string,string,string,...>    A comma-separated list of file paths specifying the product dissemination units.
                                                     Each path may contain the wildcards '**' (matches recursively any directory),
                                                     '*' (matches any character sequence in path names) and
                                                     '?' (matches any single character).
                                                     If not given, the parameter 'sourceProducts' must be provided.
  -PtargetDir=<file>                                 The directory to which the stitched product shall be written.
                                                     Within this directory, a folder of the SLSTR L1B naming format will be created.
                                                     If no target directory is given, the product will be written to the user directory.

OPERATOR: PhaseToHeight
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt PhaseToHeight [options] 

Description:
  Phase to Height conversion


Source Options:
  -SsourceProduct=<file>    Source product that contains unwrapped phase.
                            This is a mandatory source.

Parameter Options:
  -Pdegree1D=<int>       Degree of the 1D polynomial to fit reference phase through.
                         Value must be one of '1', '2', '3', '4', '5'.
                         Default value is '2'.
  -Pdegree2D=<int>       Degree of the 2D polynomial to fit reference phase through.
                         Value must be one of '1', '2', '3', '4', '5', '6', '7', '8'.
                         Default value is '5'.
  -PnHeights=<int>       Number of height samples in range [0,5000)
                         Value must be one of '2', '3', '4', '5'.
                         Default value is '3'.
  -PnPoints=<int>        Number of points for evaluation of flat earth phase at different altitudes
                         Value must be one of '100', '200', '300', '400', '500'.
                         Default value is '200'.
  -PorbitDegree=<int>    Degree of orbit (polynomial) interpolator
                         Value must be one of '2', '3', '4', '5'.
                         Default value is '3'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>PhaseToHeight</operator>
      <sources>
        <sourceProduct>${sourceProduct}</sourceProduct>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <nPoints>int</nPoints>
        <nHeights>int</nHeights>
        <degree1D>int</degree1D>
        <degree2D>int</degree2D>
        <orbitDegree>int</orbitDegree>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

OPERATOR: PixEx
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt PixEx [options] 

Description:
  Extracts pixels from given locations and source products.

Computed Properties:
PixExMeasurementReader measurements


Parameter Options:
  -PaggregatorStrategyType=<string>                  If the window size is larger than 1, this parameter describes by which method a single 
                                                     value shall be derived from the pixels.
                                                     Value must be one of 'no aggregation', 'mean', 'min', 'max', 'median'.
                                                     Default value is 'no aggregation'.
  -PcoordinatesFile=<file>                           Path to a file containing geo-coordinates. BEAM's placemark files can be used.
  -PdateInterpretationPattern=<string>               Describes how a date/time section inside a product filename should be interpreted. E.G. yyyyMMdd_HHmmss
                                                     Default value is 'yyyyMMdd'.
  -PexportBands=<boolean>                            Specifies if bands are to be exported
                                                     Default value is 'true'.
  -PexportExpressionResult=<boolean>                 If true, the expression result is exported per pixel, otherwise the expression 
                                                     is used as filter (all pixels in given window must be valid).
                                                     Default value is 'true'.
  -PexportKmz=<boolean>                              If set to true, a Google KMZ file will be created, which contains the coordinates where pixels are found.
                                                     Default value is 'false'.
  -PexportMasks=<boolean>                            Specifies if masks are to be exported
                                                     Default value is 'true'.
  -PexportSubScenes=<boolean>                        If set to true, sub-scenes of the regions, where pixels are found, are exported.
                                                     Default value is 'false'.
  -PexportTiePoints=<boolean>                        Specifies if tie-points are to be exported
                                                     Default value is 'true'.
  -Pexpression=<string>                              Band maths expression (optional). Defines valid pixels.
  -PextractTimeFromFilename=<boolean>                If set to true, the sensing start and sensing stop should be extracted from the filename of each input product.
                                                     Default value is 'false'.
  -PfilenameInterpretationPattern=<string>           Describes how the filename of a product should be interpreted.
                                                     Default value is '*${startDate}*${endDate}*'.
  -PincludeOriginalInput=<boolean>                   Determines if the original input measurements shall be included in the output.
                                                     Default value is 'false'.
  -PmatchupFile=<file>                               Path to a CSV-file containing geo-coordinates associated with measurements accordingto BEAM CSV format specification
  -PoutputDir=<file>                                 The output directory.
                                                     This is a mandatory parameter.
  -PoutputFilePrefix=<string>                        The prefix is used to name the output files.
                                                     Default value is 'pixEx'.
  -PsourceProductPaths=<string,string,string,...>    A comma-separated list of file paths specifying the source products.
                                                     Each path may contain the wildcards '**' (matches recursively any directory),
                                                     '*' (matches any character sequence in path names) and
                                                     '?' (matches any single character).
  -PsubSceneBorderSize=<int>                         An additional border around the region where pixels are found.
                                                     Default value is '0'.
  -PtimeDifference=<string>                          The acceptable time difference compared to the time given for a coordinate.
                                                     The format is a number followed by (D)ay, (H)our or (M)inute. If no time difference is provided, all input products are considered regardless of their time.
  -PwindowSize=<integer>                             Side length of surrounding window (uneven)
                                                     Default value is '1'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>PixEx</operator>
      <sources>
        <sourceProducts>${sourceProducts}</sourceProducts>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <sourceProductPaths>string,string,string,...</sourceProductPaths>
        <exportBands>boolean</exportBands>
        <exportTiePoints>boolean</exportTiePoints>
        <exportMasks>boolean</exportMasks>
        <coordinates>
          <coordinate>
            <name>string</name>
            <latitude>double</latitude>
            <longitude>double</longitude>
            <dateTime>date</dateTime>
            <originalValues>
              <originalValue>
                <variableName>string</variableName>
                <value>string</value>
              </originalValue>
              <_.002e../>
            </originalValues>
            <id>int</id>
          </coordinate>
          <_.002e../>
        </coordinates>
        <timeDifference>string</timeDifference>
        <coordinatesFile>file</coordinatesFile>
        <matchupFile>file</matchupFile>
        <windowSize>integer</windowSize>
        <outputDir>file</outputDir>
        <outputFilePrefix>string</outputFilePrefix>
        <expression>string</expression>
        <exportExpressionResult>boolean</exportExpressionResult>
        <aggregatorStrategyType>string</aggregatorStrategyType>
        <exportSubScenes>boolean</exportSubScenes>
        <subSceneBorderSize>int</subSceneBorderSize>
        <exportKmz>boolean</exportKmz>
        <extractTimeFromFilename>boolean</extractTimeFromFilename>
        <dateInterpretationPattern>string</dateInterpretationPattern>
        <filenameInterpretationPattern>string</filenameInterpretationPattern>
        <includeOriginalInput>boolean</includeOriginalInput>
        <scatterPlotVariableCombinations>
          <variableCombination>
            <originalVariableName>string</originalVariableName>
            <productVariableName>string</productVariableName>
          </variableCombination>
          <_.002e../>
        </scatterPlotVariableCombinations>
      </parameters>
    </node>
  </graph>

OPERATOR: Polarimetric-Classification
----------------------------------------
Usage:
  gpt Polarimetric-Classification [options] 

Description:
  Perform Polarimetric classification of a given product


Source Options:
  -Ssource=<file>    Sets source 'source' to <filepath>.
                     This is a mandatory source.

Parameter Options:
  -Pclassification=<string>            Sets parameter 'classification' to <string>.
                                       Value must be one of 'Cloude-Pottier', 'Cloude-Pottier Dual Pol', 'H Alpha Wishart', 'H Alpha Wishart Dual Pol', 'Freeman-Durden Wishart', 'General Wishart'.
                                       Default value is 'H Alpha Wishart'.
  -Pdecomposition=<string>             Sets parameter 'decomposition' to <string>.
                                       Value must be one of 'Sinclair Decomposition', 'Pauli Decomposition', 'Freeman-Durden Decomposition', 'Generalized Freeman-Durden Decomposition', 'Yamaguchi Decomposition', 'van Zyl Decomposition', 'H-A-Alpha Quad Pol Decomposition', 'Cloude Decomposition', 'Touzi Decomposition'.
                                       Default value is 'Sinclair Decomposition'.
  -PmaxIterations=<int>                The maximum number of iterations
                                       Valid interval is [1, 100].
                                       Default value is '3'.
  -PmixedCategoryThreshold=<double>    The threshold for classifying pixels to mixed category
                                       Valid interval is (0, *).
                                       Default value is '0.5'.
  -PnumFinalClasses=<int>              The desired number of classes
                                       Valid interval is [9, 100].
                                       Default value is '15'.
  -PnumInitialClasses=<int>            The initial number of classes
                                       Valid interval is [9, 1000].
                                       Default value is '90'.
  -PwindowSize=<int>                   The sliding window size
                                       Valid interval is (1, 100].
                                       Default value is '5'.

Graph XML Format:
  <graph id="someGraphId">
    <version>1.0</version>
    <node id="someNodeId">
      <operator>Polarimetric-Classification</operator>
      <sources>
        <source>${source}</source>
      </sources>
      <parameters>
        <classification>string</classification>
        <windowSize>int</windowSize>
        <maxIterations>int</maxIterations>
        <numInitialClasses>int</numInitialClasses>
